#########################
# BALKANS FLAVOR EVENTS #
#########################
# Events contained here are for tags that don't have enough content to justify being separated into their own modules, but have more than technical events.
# This mod is GREECE-FIRST, everything else second (yes, even Byzantium). Just because a tag is included in this mod does NOT mean that it will receive content at the level of fidelity Greece or Byzantium, although everyone will have content up to 1936 eventually.
# If you think that every country having issues with its constitution or with yeeting their monarchs is boring, take it up with them. The Balkans in the 1800s were allergic to political stability (yes this continued into the 1900s -looking at you Bosnia-).
# Certain events/effect fire from the TUR scope; this is for ease of scripting since the Ottoman State is THE constant for most Balkan crises.

####################

# For Greece content, see the "grefm" module
# For Byzantium content, see the "byzfm" module
# For Balkan Nations content, see the "balkfm" module
# For Ottoman/Turkish content, see the "turkfm" module
# For Orthodox Church content, see the "eocfm" module
# For Eastern Question content, see the "eqfm" module

####################

namespace = balkfm

# [XXX] refers to events that occur only if other mods are present and detected

	type = country_event
	placement = root
	hidden = yes

	}

	immediate = {
		balkfm_balkanize_effect = yes
	}
	
	orphan = yes
	
}

#### HIDDEN TECHNICAL EVENTS (VARIABLE CLEANUP) ####

balkfm.010 = { # The Unused Variable Dumpster Fire
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = {
		# DO NOT CALL THIS EVENT. This is here to shut up the error log.
	}

	immediate = {
		remove_global_variable = has_formed_tsar
		remove_variable = romania_subject
		set_variable = romania_unification_in_motion
		set_variable = eocfm_crusade_attacker
		set_variable = eocfm_crusade_defender
		set_global_variable = eqfm_cancel_struggle
		remove_variable = balkfm_1848_failed
		
		remove_variable = eocfm_devout_leader_var
		remove_variable = eocfm_rome_patriarch_var
		remove_variable = eocfm_constantinople_patriarch_var
		remove_variable = eocfm_antioch_patriarch_var
		remove_variable = eocfm_jerusalem_patriarch_var
		remove_variable = eocfm_alexandria_patriarch_var
		remove_variable = eocfm_moscow_patriarch_var
		remove_variable = eocfm_rome_controller_var
		remove_variable = eocfm_constantinople_controller_var
		remove_variable = eocfm_antioch_controller_var
		remove_variable = eocfm_jerusalem_controller_var
		remove_variable = eocfm_alexandria_controller_var
		remove_variable = eocfm_moscow_controller_var
		remove_global_variable = eocfm_crusade_counter
		remove_global_variable = eocfm_deposition_counter
	}
	
	orphan = yes
	
}

#### HIDDEN TECHNICAL EVENTS (VARIABLE PLACEMENT) ####

balkfm.020 = { # Places Yugoslav Secession Variable
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = {
		is_secessionist = yes
		balkfm_has_yugoslav_culture_trigger = yes
		NOT = { has_variable = balkfm_breakaway_var }
	}

	immediate = {
		set_variable = balkfm_breakaway_var
	}
	
}

#### HIDDEN TECHNICAL EVENTS (REBEL PASHA SPAWNS)

balkfm.030 = { # Creates Hersek with Smaïl-aga at the Helm; this is evaluated from MON scope
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = { 
		has_modifier = modifier_balkfm_tolerated_abuses
		NOR = { 
			has_global_variable = balkfm_smail_aga_rebelled
			exists = c:HRSK
		}
		any_character_in_void = {
			has_template = template_balkfm_cengic_smail
		}
		c:TUR ?= {
			owns_entire_state_region = STATE_BOSNIA
			has_journal_entry = je_sick_man_main # serves as a time limit
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_global_variable = balkfm_smail_aga_rebelled
		random_character_in_void = {	
			limit = {
				has_template = template_balkfm_cengic_smail
			}
			save_scope_as = balkfm_smail_aga_scope
		}
		create_country = { # Hersek with Bosnia
			tag = HRSK
			origin = c:TUR
			state = s:STATE_BOSNIA.region_state:TUR
		}
		c:HRSK = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					exists = scope:balkfm_smail_aga_scope
				}
				scope:balkfm_smail_aga_scope = {
					free_character_from_void = yes
					set_character_as_ruler = yes
				}
			}
			else = {
				create_character = {
					template = template_balkfm_cengic_smail
				}
				random_character_in_void = {
					limit = {
						has_template = template_balkfm_cengic_smail
					}
					free_character_from_void = yes
					set_character_as_ruler = yes
					save_scope_as = balkfm_smail_aga_scope
				}
			}
		}
		s:STATE_BOSNIA = {
			random_scope_state = {
				save_scope_as = bosnia_state_scope
			}
		}
		c:TUR = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = balkfm.337 # The Arrogance of Samïl-aga
			}
		}
		c:MON = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = balkfm.337 # The Arrogance of Samïl-aga
			}
			remove_modifier = modifier_balkfm_tolerated_abuses
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_journal_entry = je_eqfm_sub
			}
			post_notification = notification_balkfm_hersek_smail
		}
	}
	
}

balkfm.031 = { # Creates Hersek with Ali Pasha at the Helm
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = { # this is evaluated from MON scope
		has_global_variable = balkfm_ali_pasha_greenlight
		NOT = { 
			exists = c:HRSK
		}
		any_character_in_void = {
			has_template = template_balkfm_rizvanbegovic_ali
		}
		c:TUR ?= {
			owns_entire_state_region = STATE_BOSNIA
			has_journal_entry = je_sick_man_main # serves as a time limit
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_character_in_void = {
			limit = {
				has_template = template_balkfm_rizvanbegovic_ali
			}
			save_scope_as = balkfm_ali_pasha_scope
		}
		create_country = { # Hersek using Bosnia
			tag = HRSK
			origin = c:TUR
			state = s:STATE_BOSNIA.region_state:TUR
		}
		c:HRSK = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					exists = scope:balkfm_ali_pasha_scope
				}
				scope:balkfm_ali_pasha_scope = {
					free_character_from_void = yes
					set_character_as_ruler = yes
				}
			}
			else = {
				create_character = {
					template = template_balkfm_rizvanbegovic_ali
				}
				random_character_in_void = {
					limit = {
						has_template = template_balkfm_rizvanbegovic_ali
					}
					free_character_from_void = yes
					set_character_as_ruler = yes
					save_scope_as = balkfm_ali_pasha_scope
				}
			}
			random_scope_character = {
				limit = {
					has_template = template_balkfm_rizvanbegovic_ali
				}
				save_scope_as = balkfm_ali_pasha_scope
			}
		}
		s:STATE_BOSNIA = {
			random_scope_state = {
				save_scope_as = bosnia_state_scope
			}
		}
		c:TUR = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = balkfm.338 # The Arrogance of Ali Pasha
			}
		}
		c:MON = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = balkfm.338 # The Arrogance of Ali Pasha
			}
		}
		remove_global_variable = balkfm_ali_pasha_greenlight
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_journal_entry = je_eqfm_sub
			}
			post_notification = notification_balkfm_hersek_ali
		}
	}
	
}

#### TECHNICAL EVENTS (TUR INTERACTIONS) ####

balkfm.080 = { # Skirmishes with Montenegro
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = balkfm.080.t
	desc = balkfm.080.d
	flavor = balkfm.080.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "europenorthamerica_before_the_battle"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_military.dds"
	
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
	}
	
	immediate = {
		s:STATE_BOSNIA = {
			random_scope_state = {
				save_scope_as = bosnia_state_scope
			}
		}
		s:STATE_MONTENEGRO = {
			random_scope_state = {
				save_scope_as = montenegro_state_scope
			}
		}
		s:STATE_ALBANIA = {
			random_scope_state = {
				save_scope_as = albania_state_scope
			}
		}
		c:MON = {
			save_scope_as = montenegro_scope
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = balkfm.080.a
		default_option = yes
	}

}

balkfm.081 = { # The Schemes of Ali Pasha
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = balkfm.081.t
	desc = balkfm.081.d
	flavor = balkfm.081.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "ep1_clandestine_meeting"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_skull.dds"
	
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
	}
	
	immediate = {
		create_character = {
			template = template_balkfm_lutfi_omer
		}
		random_character_in_void = {
			limit = {
				has_template = template_balkfm_rizvanbegovic_ali
			}
			save_scope_as = ali_pasha_scope
		}
		random_character_in_void = {
			limit = {

balkfm.084 = { # The South Bessarabian Retrocession (romania.4 integrated into balkfm)
	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT
	title = balkfm.084.t
	desc = balkfm.084.d
	flavor =  balkfm.084.f

	duration = 3

	event_image = {
		video = "southamerica_aristocrats"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_default.dds"

	trigger = {
		# triggered by JE
	}

	immediate = {
        random_scope_state = {
        	limit = {
				state_region = s:STATE_BESSARABIA
        	}
        	save_scope_as = south_bessarabia_cession
        }
        random_country = {
        	limit = {
				OR = {
    				has_variable = ROM_united_principality
    				AND = {
    					is_subject = yes
    					top_overlord ?= {
    						has_variable = ROM_united_principality
    					}
    				}
    			}
        	}
        	save_scope_as = romanian_bessarabia_receiver
        }
		set_variable = balkfm_bessarabia_owner
	}

	option = { 
		name = balkfm.084.a
		default_option = yes
		s:STATE_BESSARABIA = {
			set_owner_of_provinces = {
				country = scope:romanian_bessarabia_receiver
				provinces = { xB0E0A0 x6BF7B8 x712161 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				p:x50F5CB = {
					owner = ROOT
				}
			}
			s:STATE_DOBRUDJA = {
				set_owner_of_provinces = {
					country = scope:romanian_bessarabia_receiver
					provinces = { x50F5CB }
				}
			}
		}
		change_relations = {
			country = scope:romanian_bessarabia_receiver
			value = 25
		}
		scope:romanian_bessarabia_receiver = {
			change_relations = {
				country = ROOT
				value = 25
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = balkfm.682 # Retrocession Granted
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
	}
	
	option = { 
		name = balkfm.084.b
		change_relations = {
			country = scope:romanian_bessarabia_receiver
			value = -25
		}
		scope:romanian_bessarabia_receiver = {
			change_relations = {
				country = ROOT
				value = -25
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = balkfm.683 # Retrocession Denied
			}
			
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
	}
}

	duration = 3

		any_scope_state = {
			NOT = { has_modifier = modifier_balkfm_brigandage }
		}
	}

		NOT = {
			has_journal_entry = je_balkfm_brigandage
		}
	}
	
	cooldown = {
		years = 3
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_modifier = modifier_balkfm_brigandage }
			}
			save_scope_as = brigandage_state
		}
	}

		name = balkfm.110.a
		default_option = yes
		scope:brigandage_state = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_balkfm_brigandage
				months = normal_modifier_time
			}
			add_radicals_in_state = {
				value = small_radicals
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_journal_entry = je_grefm_bavarocracy_main
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = je_grefm_bavarocracy_minus_50
				change_variable = {
					name = grefm_bavarocracy_var
					add = -50
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
}

balkfm.200 = { # Yugoslavism Starter Event
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = {
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = {
				desc = balkfm.200.t2
				trigger = {
					c:MON ?= this
				}
			}
			triggered_desc = {
				desc = balkfm.200.t3
				trigger = {
					c:SER ?= this
				}
			}
			triggered_desc = {
				desc = balkfm.200.t4
				trigger = {
					has_variable = balkfm_texas_left
				}
			}
			triggered_desc = {
				desc = balkfm.200.t1
				trigger = {
					always = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = {
				desc = balkfm.200.d2
				trigger = {
					c:MON ?= this
				}
			}
			triggered_desc = {
				desc = balkfm.200.d3
				trigger = {
					c:SER ?= this
				}
			}
			triggered_desc = {
				desc = balkfm.200.d4
				trigger = {
					has_variable = balkfm_texas_left
				}
			}
			triggered_desc = {
				desc = balkfm.200.d1
				trigger = {
					always = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	flavor = {
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = {
				desc = balkfm.200.f2
				trigger = {
					c:MON ?= this
				}
			}
			triggered_desc = {
				desc = balkfm.200.f3
				trigger = {
					c:SER ?= this
				}
			}
			triggered_desc = {
				desc = balkfm.200.f4
				trigger = {
					has_variable = balkfm_texas_left
				}
			}
			triggered_desc = {
				desc = balkfm.200.f1
				trigger = {
					always = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	event_image = {
		video = "unspecific_ruler_speaking_to_people"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_flag_yug.dds"
	
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
	}
	
	immediate = {
		balkfm_initialize_yugoslavism_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					any_character_in_void = {
						has_template = template_balkfm_garasanin_ilija
					}
				}
			}
			create_character = {
				template = template_balkfm_garasanin_ilija
				on_created = {
					place_character_in_void = 720 # 60 year lease on life
				}
			}
		}
		random_character_in_void = {
			limit = {
				has_template = template_balkfm_garasanin_ilija
			}
			save_scope_as = garasanin_scope
		}
		c:TUR = {
			save_scope_as = ottoman_scope
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = balkfm.200.a
		default_option = yes
		custom_tooltip = balkfm_yugoslavism_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					always = no ##TODO Enable this option once Montenegrin Nationalism is implemented
#					# c:MON ?= this
				}
				trigger_event = {
					id = balkfm.380 # Montenegrin Nationalism
					days = 60
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					c:SER ?= this
				}
				trigger_event = {
					id = balkfm.480 # Serbian Nationalism
					days = 60
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
#						country_has_primary_culture = cu:slovene
						country_has_primary_culture = cu:croat
					}
				}
				trigger_event = {
					id = balkfm.980 # The Triune Dream
					days = 60
				}
			}
		}
		balkfm_determine_yugoslav_leader_effect = yes
	}
	
}

balkfm.206 = { # Yugoslav Breakaways Seek Union!
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = balkfm.206.t
	desc = balkfm.206.d
	flavor = balkfm.206.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "europenorthamerica_political_extremism"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_flag_yug.dds"
	
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_global_variable = balkfm_breakaway_technical }
		has_technology_researched = pan-nationalism
		any_country = {
			has_variable = balkfm_breakaway_var
			balkfm_is_annexation_candidate_trigger = yes
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_global_variable = balkfm_breakaway_technical
		random_primary_culture = {
			save_scope_as = primary_culture_scope
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = balkfm_breakaway_var
			}
			save_scope_as = balkfm_breakaway_scope
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Annex Them
		name = balkfm.206.a
		default_option = yes
		create_incident = {
			country = scope:balkfm_breakaway_scope
			value = 10
		}
		annex = scope:balkfm_breakaway_scope
	}
	
	option = { # Nope
		name = balkfm.206.b
		change_relations = {
			country = scope:balkfm_breakaway_scope
			value = 50
		}
		scope:balkfm_breakaway_scope = {
			remove_variable = balkfm_breakaway_var
		}
	}
	
	after = {
		remove_global_variable = balkfm_breakaway_technical
	}

}

balkfm.207 = { # Yugoslav Annexation
	type = country_event
	placement = scope:balkfm_yugoslav_annex_scope
	
	title = balkfm.207.t
	desc = balkfm.207.d
	flavor = balkfm.207.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "unspecific_signed_contract"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_flag_yug.dds"
	
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		has_technology_researched = pan-nationalism
		any_country = {
			balkfm_has_yugoslav_culture_trigger = yes
			balkfm_is_annexation_candidate_trigger = yes
			relations:root >= relations_threshold:cordial
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				balkfm_has_yugoslav_culture_trigger = yes
				balkfm_is_annexation_candidate_trigger = yes
				relations:root >= relations_threshold:cordial
			}
			save_scope_as =  balkfm_yugoslav_annex_scope
		}
	}
	
	cooldown = {
		years = 2 # putting the brakes on RNGesus
	}
	
	option = { # Annex Them
		name = balkfm.207.a
		default_option = yes
		annex = scope:balkfm_yugoslav_annex_scope
	}
	
	option = { # Nope
		name = balkfm.207.b
		change_relations = {
			country = scope:balkfm_yugoslav_annex_scope
			value = 50
		}
		scope:balkfm_yugoslav_annex_scope = {
			set_variable = balkfm_annexation_declined
		}
	}

}

	type = country_event
	placement = root

	title = balkfm.209.t
	desc = balkfm.209.d
	flavor = balkfm.209.f

	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_flag_yug.dds"

	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		save_scope_as = formation_country
		cu:bosniak = {
			save_scope_as = unification_culture
		}
		cu:croat = {
			save_scope_as = unification_culture_2
		}
		cu:serb = {
			save_scope_as = unification_culture_3
		}
		cu:slovene = {
			save_scope_as = unification_culture_4
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_diplomatic_relevance = ROOT
			}
			post_notification = unification_notification_four_culture
		}
		remove_variable = balkfm_yugoslav_leader_var
	}

	option = {
		name = balkfm.209.a
		default_option = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = unification_prestige
			months = very_long_modifier_time
		}
		every_state_region = {
			limit = {
				region = sr:region_balkans
				any_scope_state = {
					NOT = { owner = ROOT }
					NOT = { has_claim_by = ROOT }
				}
			}
			add_claim = ROOT
		}
	}
	
}

			type = je_balkfm_mon_military_reform
		}

			add_modifier = modifier_balkfm_spartan_existence
		}
		show_as_tooltip = {
			add_modifier = modifier_balkfm_border_feud

		hidden_effect = {

balkfm.308 = { # The Passing of the Bishop
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = balkfm.308.t
	desc = balkfm.308.d
	flavor = balkfm.308.f
	
	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:balkfm_ruler_scope
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_skull.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		ruler = {
			has_template = template_balkfm_petrovic_petar
			has_modifier = modifier_balkfm_tuberculosis
		}
		NOT = {
			has_variable = balkfm_mon_illness_var
		}
	}
	
	cancellation_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			ruler = {
				has_template = template_balkfm_petrovic_petar
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		ruler = {
			save_scope_as = balkfm_ruler_scope
		}
		heir = {
			save_scope_as = balkfm_heir_scope
		}
		create_character = {
			template = template_balkfm_petrovic_pero
			on_created = {
				place_character_in_void = 24
			}
		}
		random_character_in_void = {
			limit = {
				has_template = template_balkfm_petrovic_pero
			}
			save_scope_as = balkfm_pero_scope
		}
		set_variable = balkfm_mon_illness_var
	}
	
	option = {
		name = balkfm.308.a
		default_option = yes
		scope:balkfm_ruler_scope = {
			kill_character = yes
		}
		trigger_event = {
			id = balkfm.310 # Old Rivalries
			days = 30
		}
	}

}

balkfm.311 = { # A Hostile Court
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = balkfm.311.t
	desc = balkfm.311.d
	flavor = balkfm.311.f
	
	gui_window = event_window_2char

	left_icon = scope:balkfm_landowners_leader_scope
	right_icon = scope:balkfm_pero_scope
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_newspaper.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/2Characters"

	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		# triggered by balkfm.310
	}
	
	cancellation_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			ruler = {
				has_template = template_balkfm_petrovic_danilo
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		ig:ig_landowners = {
			leader = {
				save_scope_as = balkfm_landowners_leader_scope
			}
		}
		random_character_in_void = {
			limit = {
				has_template = template_balkfm_petrovic_pero
			}
			save_scope_as = balkfm_pero_scope
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Respect my Authoritay
		name = balkfm.311.a
		default_option = yes
		ruler = {	
			add_modifier = modifier_balkfm_replaced_court
			set_as_interest_group_leader = yes
		}
		scope:balkfm_landowners_leader_scope = {
			exile_character = yes
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = balkfm_danilo_finna_get_shot
			years = { 9 10 } # Reigned for just over 9 years
		}
		remove_variable = balkfm_mon_illness_var
	}
	
	option = { # Be a BetaBoi
		name = balkfm.311.b
		add_modifier = modifier_balkfm_unanswered_feud
		scope:balkfm_pero_scope = {
			set_as_interest_group_leader = yes
			free_character_from_void = yes
		}
		remove_variable = balkfm_mon_illness_var
	}

}

balkfm.312 = { # Blood Revenge
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = balkfm.312.t
	desc = balkfm.312.d
	flavor = balkfm.312.f

		video = "southamerica_public_figure_assassination"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		ruler = {
			has_template = template_balkfm_petrovic_danilo
			has_modifier = modifier_balkfm_replaced_court
		}
		NOR = {
			has_variable = balkfm_danilo_finna_get_shot
			has_variable = balkfm_mon_illness_var
		}
		c:AUS = {
			relations:root < relations_threshold:cordial # the killer was rumored to be sponsored by the Austrian court
		}
	}
	
	cancellation_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			ruler = {
				has_template = template_balkfm_petrovic_danilo
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		ruler = {
			save_scope_as = balkfm_ruler_scope
		}
		heir = {
			save_scope_as = balkfm_heir_scope
		}
		set_variable = balkfm_danilo_finna_get_shot
	}
	
	option = {
		name = balkfm.312.a
		default_option = yes
		scope:balkfm_ruler_scope = {
			kill_character = yes
		}
		trigger_event = {
			id = balkfm.313 # A Worldly Leader
			days = 30
		}
		remove_variable = balkfm_danilo_finna_get_shot
	}

}

balkfm.331 = { # Negociations At Humac
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = balkfm.331.t
	desc = balkfm.331.d
	flavor = balkfm.331.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "europenorthamerica_before_the_battle"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_military.dds"
	
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		# triggered by balkfm.330
	}
	
	immediate = {
		balkfm_save_ali_pasha_scopes = yes
		c:TUR = {
			save_scope_as = ottoman_scope
		}
		c:RUS = {
			save_scope_as = balkfm_benefactor_scope
		}
	}
	
	option = { # be chill
		name = balkfm.331.a
		default_option = yes
		create_character = {
			# Jakov Daković, Lord of Grahovo and Montenegrin war hero
			first_name = Jakov
			last_name = Dakovic
			historical = yes
			age = 44 # age in 1838, when was appointed Grand Duke
			culture = cu:serb
			religion = rel:orthodox
			interest_group = ig_landowners
			ideology = ideology_royalist
			is_general = yes
			traits = {
				brave
				popular_commander
				expert_defensive_strategist
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			c:TUR = {
				trigger_event = {
					id = balkfm.080 # Skirmishes with Montenegro
				}
			}
		}
#		balkfm_minor_border_progress_loss_effect = yes
		set_global_variable = balkfm_humac_happened
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
	}
	
	option = { # get clapped
		name = balkfm.331.b
		trigger = {
			c:TUR ?= {
				has_state_in_state_region = STATE_MONTENEGRO
			}
		}
        create_diplomatic_play = {
			name = dp_petars_last_stand
			type = dp_return_state
			target_state = s:STATE_MONTENEGRO.region_state:TUR
		}
#		balkfm_minor_border_progress_gain_effect = yes
		custom_tooltip = balkfm.331.tt
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1 # MON really shouldn't go full Rambo
		}
	}

}

balkfm.337 = { # The Arrogance of Smaïl-aga
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = balkfm.337.t
	desc = balkfm.337.d
	flavor = balkfm.337.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "europenorthamerica_before_the_battle"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_military.dds"
	
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		# triggered by balkfm.030
	}
	
	cancellation_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			exists = c:HRSK
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		c:TUR = {
			save_scope_as = ottoman_scope
		}
		c:HRSK = {
			save_scope_as = hersek_scope
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = balkfm.337.a # crush his ass
		default_option = yes
		trigger = {
			this = c:TUR
		}
		create_diplomatic_play = {
			name = balkfm_pasha_rebellion
			target_country = c:HRSK
			type = dp_secession
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random_diplomatic_play = {
				limit = {
					c:TUR = {
						is_diplomatic_play_initiator = yes
					}
					c:HRSK = {
						is_diplomatic_play_target = yes
					}
				}
				add_diplomatic_play_war_support = { target = c:TUR value = 100 }
				add_diplomatic_play_war_support = { target = c:HRSK value = 100 }
				add_war_goal = {
					holder = c:TUR
					type = conquer_state
					target_state = scope:bosnia_state_scope
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 99
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = balkfm.337.b # let him go (lol wat)
		trigger = {
			this = c:TUR
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = modifier_balkfm_chickenshit
			months = long_modifier_time
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = balkfm.337.c
		trigger = {
			this = c:MON
		}
		show_as_tooltip = {
			remove_modifier = modifier_balkfm_tolerated_abuses
		}
	}

}

balkfm.341 = { # Border Villages Burned (Defender Event)
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_global_variable = balkfm_border_event_cooldown_var
		}
		global_var:balkfm_border_incursion_var != 0
	}
	
	cancellation_trigger = {
		has_global_variable = balkfm_border_conflict_resolved
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_global_variable = {
			name = balkfm_border_event_cooldown_var
			months = 10
		}
		s:STATE_MONTENEGRO = {
			add_devastation = 5
			every_scope_state = {
				add_radicals_in_state = {
					value = small_radicals
				}
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_state_in_state_region = STATE_MONTENEGRO
			}
			post_notification = notification_balkfm_villages_burned
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				global_var:balkfm_border_incursion_var = 1
			}
			c:MON = {
				balkfm_minor_border_progress_gain_effect = yes
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				global_var:balkfm_border_incursion_var = 1
			}
			c:TUR = {
				balkfm_minor_border_progress_gain_effect = yes
			}
		}
	}

}

balkfm.342 = { # Village Skirmish Escalates (Defender Event)
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = balkfm.342.t
	desc = {
		triggered_desc = {
			desc = balkfm.342.d1
			trigger = {	
				c:MON = this
			}
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			desc = balkfm.342.d2
			trigger = {	
				c:TUR = this
			}
		}
	}
	flavor = balkfm.342.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "middleeast_battlefield_trenches"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_military.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_global_variable = balkfm_border_event_cooldown_var
		}
		trigger_if = {
			limit = {
				c:MON = this
			}
			global_var:balkfm_border_incursion_var = 2
		}
		trigger_if = {
			limit = {
				c:TUR = this
			}
			global_var:balkfm_border_incursion_var = 1
		}
	}
	
	cancellation_trigger = {
		has_global_variable = balkfm_border_conflict_resolved
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_global_variable = {
			name = balkfm_border_event_cooldown_var
			months = 10
		}
		balkfm_save_border_conflict_scopes_effect = yes
	}
	
	
	## Montenegro Defender Options ##
	
	option = { # Dig In
		name = balkfm.342.a
		default_option = yes
		trigger = {
			c:MON = this
		}
		random_list = {
			5 = {
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_modifier = modifier_balkfm_fortifying_border
						}
						add = 10
					}
				}
				trigger_event = {
					id = balkfm.345 # Montenegrin Folk Hero Killed
					days = 15
				}
				c:TUR = {
					post_notification = notification_balkfm_folk_hero_killed
				}
			}
			5 = {
				c:TUR = {
					trigger_event = {
						id = balkfm.344 # Minority Population Massacred
						days = 15
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							country_has_state_religion = rel:catholic
							country_has_state_religion = rel:orthodox
						}
					}
					post_notification = notification_balkfm_orthodox_massacre
				}
			}
			10 = {
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							army_size >= 4
						}
						add = 50
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_modifier = modifier_balkfm_fortifying_border
						}
						add = 25
					}
				}
				post_notification = notification_balkfm_village_stalemate
				c:TUR = {
					post_notification = notification_balkfm_village_stalemate
					add_modifier = {
						name = modifier_balkfm_village_stalemate
						months = 6
						is_decaying = yes
					}
				}
				s:STATE_MONTENEGRO = {
					add_devastation = 5
					every_scope_state = {
						add_radicals_in_state = {
							value = small_radicals
						}
					}
				}
			}
			5 = {
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_modifier = modifier_balkfm_sponsoring_raids
						}
						add = 10
					}
				}
				trigger_event = {
					id = balkfm.346 # Ottoman Noble Captured
					days = 15
				}
			}
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = modifier_balkfm_village_stalemate
			months = 6
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Fall Back
		name = balkfm.342.b
		trigger = {
			c:MON = this
		}
		balkfm_minor_border_progress_loss_effect = yes
		add_radicals = {
			culture = cu:serb
			value = small_radicals
		}
		c:TUR = {
			post_notification = notification_balkfm_village_captured
		}
	}
	
	## Ottoman Defender Options ##
	
	option = { # Dig In

balkfm.343 = { # Border Incursion Repelled (Defender Event)
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = balkfm.343.t
	desc = balkfm.343.d
	flavor = balkfm.343.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "europenorthamerica_before_the_battle"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_military.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_global_variable = balkfm_border_event_cooldown_var
		}
		trigger_if = {
			limit = {
				c:MON = this
			}
			global_var:balkfm_border_incursion_var = 2
		}
		trigger_if = {
			limit = {
				c:TUR = this
			}
			global_var:balkfm_border_incursion_var = 1
		}
	}
	
	cancellation_trigger = {
		has_global_variable = balkfm_border_conflict_resolved
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_global_variable = {
			name = balkfm_border_event_cooldown_var
			months = 10
		}
		balkfm_save_border_conflict_scopes_effect = yes
		scope:balkfm_border_attacker_scope = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = balkfm.340 # Border Incursion Repelled (Attacker Variant)
			}
		}
		set_global_variable = {
			name = balkfm_border_incursion_var
			value = 0
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				c:MON = this
			}
			create_bidirectional_truce = {
				country = c:TUR
				months = 24
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				c:TUR = this
			}
			create_bidirectional_truce = {
				country = c:MON
				months = 24
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = balkfm.343.a
		default_option = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				c:MON = this
			}
			random_scope_state = {
				limit = {
					state_region = s:STATE_MONTENEGRO
				}
				add_modifier = {
					name = modifier_balkfm_weathered_the_storm
					months = short_modifier_time
				}
			}
			show_as_tooltip = {
				create_bidirectional_truce = {
					country = c:TUR
					months = 24
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				c:TUR = this
			}
			random_scope_state = {
				limit = {
					state_region = s:STATE_MONTENEGRO
				}
				add_modifier = {
					name = modifier_balkfm_secured_karadag_frontier
					months = short_modifier_time
				}
			}
			show_as_tooltip = {
				create_bidirectional_truce = {
					country = c:MON
					months = 24
				}
			}
		}
	}

}

	event_image = {

	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		# triggered by balkfm.342
	}
	
	cancellation_trigger = {
		has_global_variable = balkfm_border_conflict_resolved
	}
	
	immediate = {
		balkfm_save_border_conflict_scopes_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				c:MON = this
			}
			cu:turkish = {
				save_scope_as = balkfm_minority_culture
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				c:TUR = this
			}
			cu:serb = {
				save_scope_as = balkfm_minority_culture
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Put a Stop to It
		name = balkfm.344.a
		default_option = yes
		s:STATE_MONTENEGRO = {
			add_devastation = 5
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				c:MON = this
			}
			change_relations = {
				country = c:TUR
				value = -10
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_state_in_state_region = STATE_MONTENEGRO
				}
				post_notification = notification_balkfm_muslim_massacre
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				c:TUR = this
			}
			change_relations = {
				country = c:MON
				value = -10
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_state_in_state_region = STATE_MONTENEGRO
				}
				post_notification = notification_balkfm_orthodox_massacre
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Commit to the Atrocity
		name = balkfm.344.b
		s:STATE_MONTENEGRO = {
			add_devastation = 10
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				c:MON = this
			}
			create_incident = {
				country = c:TUR
				value = 10
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_state_in_state_region = STATE_MONTENEGRO
				}
				post_notification = notification_balkfm_muslim_massacre
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_balkfm_massacred_minorities
				months = normal_modifier_time
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				c:TUR = this
			}
			create_incident = {
				country = c:MON
				value = 10
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_state_in_state_region = STATE_MONTENEGRO
				}
				post_notification = notification_balkfm_orthodox_massacre
			}
			add_modifier = {

				months = normal_modifier_time
			}
		}
	}

balkfm.346 = { # Ottoman Noble Captured
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = balkfm.346.t
	desc = balkfm.346.d
	flavor = balkfm.346.f
	
	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:balkfm_new_captive_scope
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_fire.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		balkfm_mon_captured_nobles_value < 4
	}
	
	cancellation_trigger = {
		has_global_variable = balkfm_border_conflict_resolved
	}
	
	cooldown = {
		years = 2
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_variable = {
			name = balkfm_border_event_cooldown_var
			months = 8
		}
		balkfm_generate_captive_effect = yes
		random_character_in_void = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = balkfm_captive_var
			}
			save_scope_as = balkfm_new_captive_scope
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Let Them Go
		name = balkfm.346.a
		default_option = yes
		scope:balkfm_new_captive_scope = {
			free_character_from_void = yes
		}
		c:TUR = {
			post_notification = notification_balkfm_noble_released
		}
		add_radicals = {
			value = small_radicals
		}
		balkfm_minor_border_progress_loss_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = { # Lock them up
		name = balkfm.346.b
		scope:balkfm_new_captive_scope = {
			remove_variable = balkfm_captive_var
		}
		create_incident = {
			country = c:TUR
			value = 5
		}
		c:TUR = {
			post_notification = notification_balkfm_noble_captured
		}
		balkfm_minor_border_progress_gain_effect = yes
	}
	
	after = {
		balkfm_update_captive_variables_effect = yes
	}

}

		}
	}	
	
	option = { # For TUR, reject headtaking offer
		name = balkfm.350.a
		default_option = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = modifier_balkfm_retained_headtaking
			months = long_modifier_time
		}
		add_radicals = {
			culture = cu:serb
			value = medium_radicals
		}
		set_global_variable = balkfm_headtaking_rejected
		c:MON = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = balkfm.351 # Negociations On Headtaking
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # For TUR, accept headtaking offer
		name = balkfm.350.b
		add_modifier = {
			name = modifier_balkfm_abolished_headtaking
			months = normal_modifier_time
		}
		add_loyalists = {
			culture = cu:serb
			value = small_radicals
		}
		add_radicals = {
			strata = rich
			culture = cu:turkish
			value = small_radicals
		}
		set_global_variable = balkfm_headtaking_accepted
		c:MON = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = balkfm.351 # Negociations On Headtaking
			}
		}
	}
	
}

balkfm.351 = { # Negociations on Headtaking (MON)
	type = country_event
	placement = scope:balkfm_headtaking_country_scope
	
	title = balkfm.351.t
	desc = {
		triggered_desc = {
			desc = balkfm.351.d1
			trigger = {
				has_global_variable = balkfm_headtaking_rejected
			}
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			desc = balkfm.351.d2
			trigger = {
				has_global_variable = balkfm_headtaking_accepted
			}
		}
	}
	flavor = balkfm.351.f
	
	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:balkfm_headtaking_event_scope
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_newspaper.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		# triggered by balkfm_renounce_headtaking_button
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				c:TUR = this
			}
			c:MON = {
				save_scope_as = balkfm_headtaking_country_scope
				ruler = {
					save_scope_as = balkfm_headtaking_ruler_scope
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				c:MON = this
			}
			c:TUR = {
				save_scope_as = balkfm_headtaking_country_scope
				ruler = {
					save_scope_as = balkfm_headtaking_ruler_scope
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # For MON, headtaking offer rejected, retain headtaking
		name = balkfm.351.a
		default_option = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = modifier_balkfm_retained_headtaking
			months = normal_modifier_time
		}
		remove_global_variable = balkfm_headtaking_rejected
	}
	
	option = { # For MON, headtaking offer rejected, abolish unilaterally
		name = balkfm.351.b
		remove_modifier = modifier_balkfm_practicing_headtaking
		add_modifier = {
			name = modifier_balkfm_unilaterally_abolished_headtaking
			months = long_modifier_time
		}
		remove_global_variable = balkfm_headtaking_rejected
	}
	
	option = { # For MON, headtaking offer accepted
		name = balkfm.351.c
		remove_modifier = modifier_balkfm_practicing_headtaking
		add_modifier = {
			name = modifier_balkfm_abolished_headtaking
			months = normal_modifier_time
		}
		remove_global_variable = balkfm_headtaking_accepted
	}

}

	type = country_event

			}
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			desc = balkfm.353.t2
			trigger = {
				has_global_variable = balkfm_ransom_refused
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		triggered_desc = {
			desc = balkfm.353.d1
			trigger = {
				has_global_variable = balkfm_ransom_accepted
			}
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			desc = balkfm.353.d2
			trigger = {
				has_global_variable = balkfm_ransom_refused
			}
		}
	}
	flavor = balkfm.353.f
	
	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:balkfm_captive_scope
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_newspaper.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		# triggered by balkfm_captive sguis
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_character_in_void = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = balkfm_captive_event_target
			}
			save_scope_as = balkfm_captive_scope
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Accept the News
		name = balkfm.353.a
		default_option = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_variable = balkfm_ransom_accepted
			}
			scope:balkfm_captive_scope = {
				free_character_from_void = yes
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_balkfm_ransomed_noble
				months = normal_modifier_time
			}
			remove_global_variable = balkfm_ransom_accepted
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_variable = balkfm_ransom_refused
			}
			scope:balkfm_captive_scope = {
				add_modifier = {
					name = modifier_balkfm_rejected_hostage
				}
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_balkfm_ransom_failed
				months = short_modifier_time
			}
			remove_global_variable = balkfm_ransom_refused
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Cool story bro, where's my sword
		name = balkfm.353.b
		trigger = {
			has_global_variable = balkfm_ransom_refused
		}
		scope:balkfm_captive_scope = {
			kill_character = yes
		}
		create_incident = {
			country = c:TUR
			value = 10 # this is higher because you're just being vindictive here
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = modifier_balkfm_executed_noble
			months = normal_modifier_time
		}
		remove_global_variable = balkfm_ransom_refused
	}
}

balkfm.390 = { # [TECH] Creates Historical Heirs
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				ruler = {
					has_template = template_balkfm_petrovic_danilo
				}
				NOR = {
					has_variable = balkfm_heir_nikola_spawned
					exists = heir
				}
			}
			AND = {
				ruler = {
					has_template = template_balkfm_petrovic_nikola
				}
				NOR = {
					has_variable = balkfm_heir_danilo_spawned
					exists = heir
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				ruler = {
					has_template = template_balkfm_petrovic_danilo
				}
			}
			create_character = {
				template = template_balkfm_petrovic_nikola
			}
			set_variable = balkfm_heir_nikola_spawned
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ruler = {
					has_template = template_balkfm_petrovic_nikola
				}
			}
			create_character = {
				template = template_balkfm_petrovic_danilo_II
			}
			set_variable = balkfm_heir_danilo_spawned
		}
	}

}

balkfm.401 = { # A Constitution Imposed
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = balkfm.401.t
	desc = balkfm.401.d
	flavor = balkfm.401.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "unspecific_signed_contract"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_newspaper.dds"
	
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		has_variable = balkfm_constitution_pending
		year = 1838
	}
	
	immediate = {
		ruler = {
			save_scope_as = milos_scope
		}
		heir = {
			save_scope_as = milan_scope
		}
		remove_variable = balkfm_constitution_pending
		
	}
	
	option = {
		name = balkfm.401.a
		default_option = yes
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = balkfm.401.tt
			hidden_effect = {
				scope:milos_scope = {
					place_character_in_void = 150 # characters will expire after 15 years
				}
			}
		}
		scope:milan_scope = {
			free_character_from_void = yes
			set_character_as_ruler = yes # this feels pedantic, but he was technically Prince for 26 days
		}
		activate_law = law_type:law_wealth_voting
		activate_law = law_type:law_tenant_farmers
		activate_law = law_type:law_appointed_bureaucrats
		balkfm_minor_dynasty_support_loss_effect = yes
		trigger_event = {
			id = balkfm.402 # An Inexperienced Ruler
			days = 30
		}
		call_election = {
			months = 1
		}
		set_variable = balkfm_milos_bailed_out
	}

}

balkfm.407 = { # Defenders of the Constitution
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = balkfm.407.t
	desc = balkfm.407.d
	flavor = balkfm.407.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "europenorthamerica_political_extremism"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_newspaper.dds"
	
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		has_variable = balkfm_milos_bailed_out
		NOT = {
			has_variable = balkfm_constitution_pending
		}
		
		var:balkfm_obrenovic_support_var < 50
	}
	
	immediate = {
		ruler = {
			save_scope_as = mihailo_scope
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_scope_character = {
					has_template = template_balkfm_karadordevic_aleksander
				}
			}				
			random_scope_character = {
				limit = {
					has_template = template_balkfm_karadordevic_aleksander
				}
				save_scope_as = kaykay_scope
			}
		}
		else = {
			create_character = {
				template = template_balkfm_karadordevic_aleksander
				on_created = {
					place_character_in_void = 12
				}
			}
			random_character_in_void = {
				limit = {
					has_template = template_balkfm_karadordevic_aleksander
				}
				save_scope_as = kaykay_scope
			}
		}
		remove_variable = balkfm_milos_bailed_out
	}	
	
	option = {
		name = balkfm.407.a
		default_option = yes
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = balkfm.407.tt1
			hidden_effect = {
				scope:mihailo_scope = {
					place_character_in_void = 150 # characters will expire after 15 years
					set_variable = balkfm_obrenovic_tracker
				}
			}
		}
		scope:kaykay_scope = {
			free_character_from_void = yes
			set_character_as_ruler = yes
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = balkfm_obrenovic_wipeout
			hidden_effect = {
				set_variable = {
					name = balkfm_obrenovic_support_var
					value = 0
				}
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = balkfm.407.tt2
			hidden_effect = {
				set_variable = {
					name = balkfm_karadordevic_support_var
					value = 200
				}
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = balkfm_leading_dynasty_var
			value = 200
		}
		add_journal_entry = {
			type = je_balkfm_ser_defenders
		}
		add_journal_entry = {
			type = je_balkfm_state_reform
		}
		create_character = {
			template = template_balkfm_petronijevic_avram
			on_created = {
				add_character_role = agitator
			}
		}

	}

}

balkfm.410 = { # House Karađorđević Takes the Throne
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = balkfm.410.t
	desc = balkfm.410.d
	flavor = balkfm.410.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "votp_monarch_holding_court"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_serbia.dds"
	
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		var:balkfm_leading_dynasty_var < 1
		balkfm_has_obrenovic_ruler_trigger = yes
	}
	
	cooldown = {
		years = 1
	}
	
	immediate = {
		ruler = {
			save_scope_as = balkfm_ruler_scope
		}
		heir = {
			save_scope_as = balkfm_heir_scope
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_character_in_void = {
					has_variable = balkfm_karadordevic_tracker
				}
			}
			random_character_in_void = {
				limit = {
					has_variable = balkfm_karadordevic_tracker
				}
				save_scope_as = balkfm_karadordevic_scope
			}
		}
		else = {
			create_character = {
				template = template_balkfm_karadordevic_dynamic
				on_created = {
					set_variable = balkfm_karadordevic_tracker
					place_character_in_void = 12
				}
			}
			random_character_in_void = {
				limit = {
					has_variable = balkfm_karadordevic_tracker
				}
				save_scope_as = balkfm_karadordevic_scope
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = balkfm.410.a
		default_option = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = modifier_balkfm_royal_turmoil
			months = short_modifier_time
			is_decaying = yes
		}
		scope:balkfm_karadordevic_scope = {
			set_character_as_ruler = yes
			remove_variable = balkfm_karadordevic_tracker
		}
		scope:balkfm_ruler_scope = {
			set_variable = balkfm_obrenovic_tracker
			place_character_in_void = 150 # characters will expire after 15 years
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				exists = scope:balkfm_heir_scope
			}
			scope:balkfm_heir_scope = {
				disinherit_character = yes
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = balkfm_karadordevic_support_var
			value = 200
		}	
		set_variable = {
			name = balkfm_obrenovic_support_var
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = balkfm_leading_dynasty_var
			value = 200
		}
	}
	
}

balkfm.412 = { # Austria/Russia Requests Primacy
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = balkfm.412.t
	desc = balkfm.412.d
	flavor = balkfm.412.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "unspecific_ruler_speaking_to_people"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_default.dds"
	
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				balkfm_has_karadordevic_ruler_trigger = yes
				NOT = {
					has_variable = balkfm_russia_consul_var
				}
				c:RUS ?= {
					relations:root >= relations_threshold:cordial
				}
			}
			AND = {
				balkfm_has_obrenovic_ruler_trigger = yes
				NOT = {
					has_variable = balkfm_austria_consul_var
				}
				c:AUS ?= {
					relations:root >= relations_threshold:cordial
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = balkfm_russia_consul_var
			}
			c:RUS ?= {
				save_scope_as = balkfm_consul_scope
			}
			c:AUS ?= {
				save_scope_as = balkfm_supplicant_scope
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = balkfm_austria_consul_var
			}
			c:RUS ?= {
				save_scope_as = balkfm_supplicant_scope
			}
			c:AUS ?= {
				save_scope_as = balkfm_consul_scope
			}
		}
	}
	
	cooldown = {
		years = 5
	}
	
	option = { # Retain Current Order of Precedence
		name = balkfm.412.a 
		default_option = yes
		change_relations = {
			country = scope:balkfm_consul_scope
			value = 25
		}
		create_diplomatic_catalyst = {
			type = catalyst_relations_level_increased
			target = scope:balkfm_consul_scope
		}
		change_relations = {
			country = scope:balkfm_supplicant_scope
			value = -25
		}
		create_diplomatic_catalyst = {
			type = catalyst_diplomatic_incident
			target = scope:balkfm_supplicant_scope
		}
		balkfm_minor_dynasty_support_loss_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = { # Adopt New Order of Precedence
		name = balkfm.412.b
		add_modifier = {
			name = modifier_balkfm_diplomatic_disorder
			months = short_modifier_time
		}
		change_relations = {
			country = scope:balkfm_supplicant_scope
			value = 25
		}
		create_diplomatic_catalyst = {
			type = catalyst_relations_level_increased
			target = scope:balkfm_supplicant_scope
		}
		change_relations = {
			country = scope:balkfm_consul_scope
			value = -25
		}
		create_diplomatic_catalyst = {
			type = catalyst_diplomatic_incident
			target = scope:balkfm_consul_scope
		}
		balkfm_minor_dynasty_support_gain_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = balkfm_russia_consul_var
			}
			remove_variable = balkfm_russia_consul_var
			set_variable = balkfm_austria_consul_var
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = balkfm_austria_consul_var
			}
			remove_variable = balkfm_austria_consul_var
			set_variable = balkfm_russia_consul_var
		}
	}

}

balkfm.413 = { # Plague Outbreak!
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = balkfm.413.t
	desc = balkfm.413.d
	flavor = balkfm.413.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "southamerica_war_civilians"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_skull.dds"
	
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { 
			has_variable = balkfm_belgrade_plague_var
		}
		NOT = {
			has_variable = balkfm_constitution_pending
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_variable = balkfm_belgrade_plague_var
		c:TUR = {
			save_scope_as = ottoman_scope
		}
	}	
	
	option = {
		name = balkfm.413.a
		default_option = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = modifier_balkfm_mitigated_plague
			months = short_modifier_time
		}
		change_relations = {
			country = c:TUR
			value = -20
		}
		create_diplomatic_catalyst = {
			type = catalyst_relations_level_decreased
			target = c:TUR
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = balkfm.413.b
		add_modifier = {
			name = modifier_balkfm_plague_outbreak
			months = short_modifier_time
		}
		balkfm_minor_dynasty_support_loss_effect = yes
	}
}

balkfm.484 = { # May Assembly
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = balkfm.484.t
	desc = balkfm.484.d
	flavor = balkfm.484.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "europenorthamerica_political_extremism"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_fire.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_global_variable = balkfm_may_assembly_happened
		}
		OR = {
			owns_entire_state_region = STATE_BANAT
			owns_entire_state_region = STATE_DELVIDEK
		}
		any_scope_state ={
			OR = {
				state_region = s:STATE_BANAT
				state_region = s:STATE_DELVIDEK
			}
			radical_fraction = {
				culture = cu:serb
				value >= 0.20
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_global_variable = balkfm_may_assembly_happened
		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_entire_state_region = STATE_BANAT
				owns_entire_state_region = STATE_DELVIDEK
			}
			create_country = {
				tag = SER_VOJ
				origin = this
				state = s:STATE_BANAT.region_state:AUS
				state = s:STATE_DELVIDEK.region_state:AUS
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				owns_entire_state_region = STATE_BANAT
			}
			create_country = {
				tag = SER_VOJ
				origin = this
				state = s:STATE_BANAT.region_state:AUS
			}
		}
		else = {
			create_country = {
				tag = SER_VOJ
				origin = this
				state = s:STATE_DELVIDEK.region_state:AUS
			}
		}
		c:SER_VOJ = {
			save_scope_as = vojvodina_scope
			create_character = {
				template = template_balkfm_supljikac_stevan
			}
			create_character = {
				template = template_balkfm_rajacic_josif
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_diplomatic_relevance = c:AUS
			}
			create_bidirectional_truce = {  
				country = c:SER_VOJ  
				months = 6
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Go Pound Sand
		name = balkfm.484.a
		default_option = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			end_truce = c:SER_VOJ
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				c:SER_VOJ = {
					owns_entire_state_region = STATE_BANAT
					owns_entire_state_region = STATE_DELVIDEK
				}
			}
			create_diplomatic_play = {
				name = dp_vojvodina_uprising
				target_state = s:STATE_BANAT.region_state:SER_VOJ
				type = dp_annex_war
				add_war_goal = {
					holder = root
					type = conquer_state
					target_state = s:STATE_DELVIDEK.region_state:SER_VOJ
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				c:SER_VOJ = {
					owns_entire_state_region = STATE_BANAT
				}
			}
			create_diplomatic_play = {
				name = dp_vojvodina_uprising
				target_state = s:STATE_BANAT.region_state:SER_VOJ
				type = dp_annex_war
			}
		}
		else = {
			create_diplomatic_play = {
				name = dp_vojvodina_uprising
				target_state = s:STATE_DELVIDEK.region_state:SER_VOJ
				type = dp_annex_war
			}
		}
		c:SER = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = balkfm.485 # The Vojvodina Uprising
			}
		}
		change_infamy = -10
	}
	
	option = { # Grant Them Autonomy
		name = balkfm.484.b
		create_diplomatic_pact = {
			country = c:SER_VOJ
			type = personal_union
		}
		c:SER = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = balkfm.486 # The Serbian Voivodship
			}
		}
	}

}

balkfm.485 = { # The Vojvodina Uprising
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = balkfm.485.t
	desc = balkfm.485.d
	flavor = balkfm.485.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "europenorthamerica_political_extremism"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_fire.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		# triggered by balkfm.484
	}
	
	cancellation_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			exists = c:SER_VOJ
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		c:SER_VOJ = {
			save_scope_as = vojvodina_scope
		}
		random_diplomatic_play = {
			limit = {
				initiator = {
					c:AUS = this
				}
				target = {
					c:SER_VOJ = this
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = vojvodina_uprising_scope
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Join the War
		name = balkfm.485.a
		scope:vojvodina_uprising_scope = {
			add_target_backers = { root }
		}
		scope:vojvodina_scope = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_balkfm_serbian_supporters
				months = short_modifier_time
			}
		}
		add_loyalists = {
			culture = cu:serb
			value = very_large_radicals
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Provide Funding
		name = balkfm.485.b
		default_option = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = modifier_balkfm_aiding_vojvodina
			months = short_modifier_time
		}
		scope:vojvodina_scope = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_balkfm_serbian_supporters
				months = short_modifier_time
			}
		}
		create_incident = {
			country = c:AUS
			value = 10
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Stay Neutral
		name = balkfm.485.c
		change_relations = {
			country = scope:vojvodina_scope
			value = -50
		}
		add_radicals = {
			culture = cu:serb
			value = medium_radicals
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				country_rank >= rank_value:great_power
				has_diplomatic_relevance = c:AUS
			}
			change_relations = {
				country = c:SER
				value = 15
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				balkfm_has_obrenovic_ruler_trigger = yes
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = balkfm_obrenovic_vojvodina_tt
				hidden_effect = {
					set_variable = balkfm_obrenovic_vojvodina_var
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				balkfm_has_karadordevic_ruler_trigger = yes
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = balkfm_karadordevic_vojvodina_tt
				hidden_effect = {
					set_variable = balkfm_karadordevic_vojvodina_var
				}
			}
		}
	}

}

#### MISCELLANEOUS & TECHNICAL EVENTS ####

balkfm.490 = { # Disruptive Influence
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = balkfm.490.t
	desc = balkfm.490.d
	flavor = balkfm.490.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "southamerica_aristocrats"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_skull.dds"
	
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		has_global_variable = balkfm_humac_happened # set by balkfm.331 (Negociations at Humac)
		exists = c:MON
	}
	
	immediate = {
		remove_global_variable = balkfm_humac_happened
		balkfm_save_ali_pasha_scopes = yes
		c:MON = {
			save_scope_as = montenegro_scope
			ruler = {
				save_scope_as = montenegro_ruler_scope
			}
		}
		s:STATE_NORTHERN_SERBIA = {
			random_scope_state = {
				save_scope_as = northern_serbia_state_scope
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # stir the pot
		name = balkfm.490.a
		default_option = yes
		change_relations = {
			country = c:MON
			value = 20
		}
		set_global_variable = balkfm_stabby_stabby # triggers balkfm.332 (Knives in the Dark)
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				trigger = {
					c:MON ?= {
						relations:root < relations_threshold:neutral
					}
				}
				add = -10
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # do nothing
		name = balkfm.490.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				trigger = {
					c:MON ?= {
						relations:root < relations_threshold:neutral
					}
				}
				add = 10
			}
		}
	}

}

#### THE BATTENBURG MONARCHY ####


balkfm.500 = { # The Golden Lion Awakens
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = balkfm.500.t
	desc = balkfm.500.d
	flavor = balkfm.500.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "balkfm_bulgaria_intro"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_bulgaria.dds"
	
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
	}
	
	immediate = {
		c:TUR = {
			save_scope_as = ottoman_scope
		}
		c:RUS = {
			save_scope_as = russia_scope
		}
		ruler = {
			save_scope_as = balkfm_alex_scope
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = balkfm_coup_var
			value = 120 # Alexander had 87 months before the coup, I'm being generous here
		}
		set_global_variable = balkfm_lion_awakened
	}
	
	option = {
		name = balkfm.500.a
		default_option = yes
		add_journal_entry = {
			type = je_balkfm_bul_battenburg_monarchy
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = modifier_balkfm_national_awakening
			months = normal_modifier_time
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = balkfm.512 # Strategic Demands
				days = 180
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_variable = eocfm_is_autocephalous
					}
				}
				trigger_event = {
					id = balkfm.560 # Threats of Schism
					days = 240
				}
			}
		}
	}

}

balkfm.501 = { # Democratic Obstructions
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = balkfm.501.t
	desc = balkfm.501.d
	flavor = balkfm.501.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "unspecific_politicians_arguing"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_scales.dds"
	
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { 
			has_variable = balkfm_bulgaria_consitution_1
		}
		var:balkfm_coup_var <= 104 # Second Session of the National Assembly, relative to Alexander I's ascent to the throne
		NOT = {
			has_law = law_type:law_autocracy
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_variable = balkfm_bulgaria_consitution_1
	}

	cancellation_trigger = {
		has_law = law_type:law_oligarchy
	}

	option = { # yeet the law
		name = balkfm.501.a
		default_option = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOR = {
					has_law = law_type:law_autocracy
					has_law = law_type:law_oligarchy
				}
			}
			activate_law = law_type:law_oligarchy
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_law = law_type:law_oligarchy
			}
			activate_law = law_type:law_autocracy
		}
		add_radicals = {
			pop_type = academics
			value = very_large_radicals
		}
		add_radicals = {
			pop_type = officers
			value = very_large_radicals
		}
		add_loyalists = {
			strata = poor
			value = medium_radicals
		}
		change_relations = {
			country = c:RUS
			value = 20
		}
		custom_tooltip = balkfm_countercoup_reduce_2
	}
	
	option = { # protect the constitution
		name = balkfm.501.b
		add_modifier = {
			name = modifier_balkfm_honorable_regime
			months = long_modifier_time
		}
		add_radicals = {
			strata = rich
			value = large_radicals
		}
		change_relations = {
			country = c:RUS
			value = -20
		}
	}

}

	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_variable = balkfm_bulgaria_consitution_2 }
		var:balkfm_coup_var <= 96 # Consitution was abrogated May 9th, 1881; dissident newpapers were supressed shortly thereafter
		OR = {
			has_law = law_type:law_protected_speech
			has_law = law_type:law_right_of_assembly
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_variable = balkfm_bulgaria_consitution_2
	}	
	
	cancellation_trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_law = law_type:law_censorship
			has_law = law_type:law_outlawed_dissent
		}
	}	
	
	option = { # censor the press
		name = balkfm.502.a
		default_option = yes
		activate_law = law_type:law_censorship
		add_modifier = {
			name = modifier_balkfm_conservative_tilt

		}

			strata = poor
			value = medium_radicals
		}
		custom_tooltip = balkfm_countercoup_reduce_1
	}
	
	option = { # defend free speech

			name = modifier_balkfm_honorable_ruler
			months = normal_modifier_time
		}
		add_radicals = {

				arrogant
				hedonist

			}
		}
		create_character = {
			# Alexander von Kaulbars, Russian attache to Bulgaria
			first_name = Alexander
			last_name = Kaulbars
			historical = yes
			age = 38 # age in 1882
			culture = cu:russian
			religion = rel:orthodox

		}

		}

			country = c:TUR
			value = -25

		}

			country = c:AUS
			value = 25
		}

		}

			}

balkfm.509 = { # The August Coup
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = balkfm.509.t
	desc = balkfm.509.d
	flavor = balkfm.509.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "europenorthamerica_political_extremism"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_protest.dds"
	
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		var:balkfm_coup_var <= 0
		NOT = {
			has_variable = balkfm_august_coup_happened
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		balkfm_create_bulgarian_regency_characters = yes
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				has_template = template_balkfm_battenburg_alexander
			}
			save_scope_as = balkfm_alex_scope
		}
		heir = {
			save_scope_as = balkfm_heir_scope
		}
		ig:ig_armed_forces = {
			leader = {
				save_scope_as = balkfm_sava_scope
			}
		}
		set_variable = balkfm_august_coup_happened
	}
	
	option = { 
		name = balkfm.509.a
		default_option = yes
		scope:balkfm_alex_scope = {
			place_character_in_void = 600
		}
		hidden_effect = {	
			if = {
				limit = {
					exists = scope:balkfm_heir_scope
				}
				scope:balkfm_heir_scope = {
					kill_character = yes
				}
			}
		}
		scope:balkfm_sava_scope = {
			set_character_as_ruler = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = modifier_balkfm_russian_attaches
			}
			remove_modifier = modifier_balkfm_russian_attaches
		}
		set_variable = balkfm_alex_yeeted
	}

}

		}

			value = medium_radicals
		}
	}

	}

#### STAMBOLOVISM EVENTS ####

balkfm.520 = { # An Elected Prince
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = balkfm.520.t
	desc = balkfm.520.d
	flavor = balkfm.520.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "unspecific_politicians_arguing"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_newspaper.dds"
	
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
	}
	
	immediate = {
		balkfm_create_bulgarian_royals = yes
		random_character_in_void = {
			limit = {
				has_template = template_balkfm_sakskoburggotski_ferdinand
			}
			save_scope_as = balkfm_ferdinand_scope
		}
		random_character_in_void = {
			limit = {
				has_template = template_balkfm_dadiani_nikoloz
			}
			save_scope_as = balkfm_nikoloz_scope
		}
		random_character_in_void = {
			limit = {
				has_template = template_balkfm_bogoridi_alexander
			}
			save_scope_as = balkfm_bogoridi_scope
		}
		random_character_in_void = {
			limit = {
				has_template = template_balkfm_glucksburg_valdemar
			}
			save_scope_as = balkfm_valdemar_scope
		}
		random_character_in_void = {
			limit = {
				has_template = template_balkfm_goltz_wilhelm
			}
			save_scope_as = balkfm_goltz_scope
		}
		
		c:RUS = {
			save_scope_as = russia_scope
		}
		c:TUR = {
			save_scope_as = ottoman_scope
		}
		trigger_event = {
			id = balkfm.522 # Legitimizing the King
			days = 150
		}
		trigger_event = {
			id = balkfm.523 # Military Conciliation
			days = 240
		}
		trigger_event = {
			id = balkfm.562 # Ecclesiatic Hostility
			days = 300
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = modifier_turkfm_order_of_osmanieh
			}
			remove_modifier = modifier_turkfm_order_of_osmanieh
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Ferdinand I, the historical option
		name = balkfm.520.1
		default_option = yes
		scope:balkfm_ferdinand_scope = {
			free_character_from_void = yes
			set_character_as_ruler = yes
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Niko I Dadiani, former Prince of Mingrelia
		name = balkfm.520.2
		trigger = {
			exists = c:RUS
			OR = {
				has_diplomatic_pact = {
					who = c:RUS
					type = alliance
				}
				is_subject_of = c:RUS
			}
		}
		scope:balkfm_nikoloz_scope = {
			free_character_from_void = yes
			set_character_as_ruler = yes
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Alexander Bogoridi, former Governor-General of Rumelia
		name = balkfm.520.3
		trigger = {
			c:ERUM ?= {
				is_subject_of = root
			}
			exists = scope:balkfm_bogoridi_scope
		}
		scope:balkfm_bogoridi_scope = {
			free_character_from_void = yes
			set_character_as_ruler = yes
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Valdemar of Glucksburg, brother to King George I of Greece
		name = balkfm.520.4
		trigger = {
			exists = c:DEN
			OR = {
				has_diplomatic_pact = {
					who = c:DEN
					type = alliance
				}
				is_subject_of = c:DEN
			}
		}
		scope:balkfm_valdemar_scope = {
			free_character_from_void = yes
			set_character_as_ruler = yes
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Wilhelm von der Goltz, Prussian general who was pivotal in modernizing the Turkish army
		name = balkfm.520.5
		trigger = {
			exists = c:PRU
			OR = {
				has_diplomatic_pact = {
					who = c:PRU
					type = alliance
				}
				is_subject_of = c:PRU
			}
		}
		scope:balkfm_valdemar_scope = {
			free_character_from_void = yes
			set_character_as_ruler = yes
		}
	}	
	
	after = {
		trigger_event = {
			id = balkfm.521 # A Foreigner in Sofia
			days = 45
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			heir ?= {
				kill_character = yes # for good measure
			}
		}
		set_variable = balkfm_ferdinand_era
	}

}

	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = balkfm.521.t
	desc = {

			desc = balkfm.521.d1
			trigger = {

					has_template = template_balkfm_sakskoburggotski_ferdinand
				}
			}
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			desc = balkfm.521.d2

					has_template = template_balkfm_dadiani_nikoloz

			}

	}

	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		# triggered by balkfm.520
	}
	
	cancellation_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_variable = balkfm_ferdinand_era
		}
	}

			save_scope_as = balkfm_ferdinand_scope
		}

		}
	}

balkfm.523 = { # Military Conciliation
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = balkfm.523.t
	desc = balkfm.523.d
	flavor = balkfm.523.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "europenorthamerica_capitalists_meeting"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_sakskoburggotski.dds"
	
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		# triggered by balkfm.520
	}
	
	cancellation_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_variable = balkfm_ferdinand_era
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		ig:ig_armed_forces = {
			save_scope_as = armed_forces_scope
			leader = {
				save_scope_as = armed_forces_leader_scope
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Extend an olive branch
		name = balkfm.523.a
		default_option = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = modifier_balkfm_unchallenged_rule
			months = normal_modifier_time
		}
		scope:armed_forces_scope = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_balkfm_military_reconciliation
				months = normal_modifier_time
			}
		}
		scope:armed_forces_leader_scope = {
			set_ideology = ideology:ideology_royalist
		}
		trigger_event = {
			id = balkfm.524 # Military Insufficiency
			days = 30
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = balkfm_stamobolov_plus_1
			hidden_effect = {
				set_variable = balkfm_battenburg_letter
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Send them packing
		name = balkfm.523.b
		add_modifier = {
			name = modifier_balkfm_unchallenged_rule
			months = normal_modifier_time
		}
		scope:armed_forces_scope = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_balkfm_military_tension
				months = normal_modifier_time
			}
		}
		scope:armed_forces_leader_scope = {
			set_ideology = ideology:ideology_republican
		}
		trigger_event = {
			id = balkfm.524 # Military Insufficiency
			days = 30
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = balkfm_stamobolov_plus_1
			hidden_effect = {
				set_variable = balkfm_battenburg_letter
			}
		}
	}

}

balkfm.527 = { # Funerary Politics
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = balkfm.527.t
	desc = balkfm.527.d
	flavor = balkfm.527.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "votp_monarch_holding_court"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_portrait.dds"
	
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_variable = balkfm_ernest_coburg_died
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				exists = c:GER
			}
			c:GER = {
				save_scope_as = prussia_scope
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				exists = c:PRU
			}
			c:PRU = {
				save_scope_as = prussia_scope
			}
		}
		else = {
			random_country = {
				limit = {
					country_has_primary_culture = cu:north_german
				}
				save_scope_as = prussia_scope
			}
		}
		set_variable = balkfm_ernest_coburg_died
	}
	
	option = { # Be Whimpy
		name = balkfm.527.a
		default_option = yes
		ruler = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_balkfm_whimpy_ruler
				months = normal_modifier_time
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = balkfm_stamobolov_minus_2
			hidden_effect = {
				set_variable = balkfm_put_away_regalia
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Strut Yo Stuff
		name = balkfm.527.b
		create_incident = {
			country = scope:prussia_scope
			value = 5
		}
		ruler = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_balkfm_bold_ruler
				months = normal_modifier_time
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = balkfm_stamobolov_plus_1
			hidden_effect = {
				set_variable = balkfm_showed_off_regalia
			}
		}
	}

}

#### REIGN OF FERDINAND I EVENTS ####

balkfm.530 = { # The University of Sofia
	type = country_event
	placement = scope:university_state
	
	title = balkfm.530.t
	desc = balkfm.530.d
	flavor = balkfm.530.f
	
	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:university_benefactor
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_portrait.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		morgenrote_is_active = no
		NOT = { has_variable = balkfm_sofia_university_considered }
		has_variable = balkfm_ferdinand_era
		has_technology_researched = academia
		owns_entire_state_region = STATE_BULGARIA
	}
	
	immediate = {
		ruler = { 
			save_scope_as = university_benefactor
		}
		s:STATE_BULGARIA = {
			random_scope_state = {
				save_scope_as = university_state
			}
		}
		set_variable = balkfm_sofia_university_considered
	}
	
	option = {
		name = balkfm.530.a
		default_option = yes
		scope:university_state = {
			create_building = {
 				building = "building_university"
				level = 1
 			}
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = modifier_grefm_funding_royal_university
			months = normal_modifier_time
			multiplier = money_amount_multiplier_small
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = balkfm.530.b
		scope:university_benefactor = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_grefm_blocked_building_university
				months = normal_modifier_time
			}
		}
	}

}

balkfm.531 = { # Royal Recognition
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = balkfm.531.t
	desc = balkfm.531.d
	flavor = balkfm.531.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "ep1_power_blocs"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_portrait.dds"
	
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		# triggered by je_balkfm_bul_stambolovism
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				has_template = template_balkfm_stambolov_stefan
			}
			save_scope_as = stambolov_scope
		}
		create_character = {
			template = template_balkfm_stoilov_constantin
			on_created = {
				place_character_in_void = 12
			}
		}
		random_character_in_void = {
			limit = {
				has_template = template_balkfm_stoilov_constantin
			}
			save_scope_as = stoilov_scope
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Dismiss Stambolov
		name = balkfm.531.a
		default_option = yes
		trigger = {
			exists = scope:stambolov_scope
		}
		scope:stambolov_scope = {
			place_character_in_void = 12
		}
		scope:stoilov_scope = {
			set_as_interest_group_leader = yes
			free_character_from_void = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_technology_researched = nationalism
					NOR = {
						owns_entire_state_region = STATE_SKOPIA
						owns_entire_state_region = STATE_MACEDONIA
					}
				}
				trigger_event = {
					id = balkfm.529 # Severed Hands
					days = 200
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ruler = {
					has_template = template_balkfm_sakskoburggotski_ferdinand
				}
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_balkfm_foxy_ferdinand
				months = long_modifier_time
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_balkfm_royal_recognition
				months = long_modifier_time
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Keep Stambolov
		name = balkfm.531.b
		trigger = {
			exists = scope:stambolov_scope
		}
		scope:stambolov_scope = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_balkfm_bulgarian_bismark
				months = long_modifier_time
			}
		}
		scope:stoilov_scope = {
			set_as_interest_group_leader = yes
			free_character_from_void = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ruler = {
					has_template = template_balkfm_sakskoburggotski_ferdinand
				}
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_balkfm_foxy_ferdinand
				months = long_modifier_time
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_balkfm_royal_recognition
				months = long_modifier_time
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Generic Option in case Stambolov isn't around
		name = balkfm.531.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				exists = scope:stambolov_scope
			}
		}
		scope:stoilov_scope = {
			set_as_interest_group_leader = yes
			free_character_from_void = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ruler = {
					has_template = template_balkfm_sakskoburggotski_ferdinand
				}
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_balkfm_foxy_ferdinand
				months = long_modifier_time
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_balkfm_royal_recognition
				months = long_modifier_time
			}
		}
	}
	
	after = {	
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_subject_of = c:TUR
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = balkfm.532 # Spring in Constantinople
			}
		}
	}

}

	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = balkfm.558.t
	desc = {

			trigger = {
				is_subject = yes
			}
		}
		triggered_desc {
			desc = balkfm.558.d2
			trigger = {
				is_subject = no
			}
		}
	}
	flavor = {
		triggered_desc {
			desc = balkfm.558.f1
			trigger = {
				is_subject = yes
			}
		}
		triggered_desc {
			desc = balkfm.558.f2
			trigger = {
				is_subject = no
			}
		}
	}
	
	event_image = {
		video = "ep1_transfer_of_authority"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_bulgaria.dds"
	
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		# triggered by je_balkfm_bul_millet
	}
	
	immediate = {
		c:TUR = {
			save_scope_as = ottoman_scope
		}
		overlord ?= {
			save_scope_as = balkfm_overlord_scope
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = balkfm_backing_bulgaria
			}
			save_scope_as = balkfm_support_scope
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = balkfm.558.a
		default_option = yes
		set_country_type = recognized
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:balkfm_overlord_scope ?= {
					c:TUR ?= this
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				make_independent = yes
			}
			scope:balkfm_overlord_scope = {
				create_diplomatic_pact = {
					type = protectorate
					country = root
				}
			}
		}
		change_tag = BUL
		add_primary_culture = cu:bulgarian
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_has_primary_culture = cu:turkish
			}
			remove_primary_culture = cu:turkish
		}
		set_state_religion = rel:orthodox
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = balkfm.558.tt # vanilla loc is broken here. I can't be assed to track down the problem.
			ig:ig_devout = { # this mimics the game setup effect for Orthodox nations
				set_interest_group_name = ig_orthodox_church
				remove_ideology = ideology_patriarchal
				add_ideology = ideology_orthodox_patriarch
			}
		}
		trigger_event = {
			id = balkfm.559 # Securing our Sovereignty
			days = 30
		}
	}

}

	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = balkfm.559.t

	}
