		# triggered by balkfm.558
	}
	
	immediate = {
		create_character = {
			template = template_balkfm_battenburg_alexander
			on_created = {
				place_character_in_void = 12
			}
		}
		create_character = {
			template = template_balkfm_bogoridi_emmanuel
			on_created = {
				place_character_in_void = 12
			}
		}
		create_character = {
			template = template_balkfm_exarch_alexander
			on_created = {
				place_character_in_void = 12
			}
		}
		random_character_in_void = {
			limit = {
				has_template = template_balkfm_battenburg_alexander
			}
			save_scope_as = balkfm_battenburg_scope
		}
		random_character_in_void = {
			limit = {
				has_template = template_balkfm_bogoridi_emmanuel
			}
			save_scope_as = balkfm_bogoridi_scope
		}
		random_character_in_void = {
			limit = {
				has_template = template_balkfm_exarch_alexander
			}
			save_scope_as = balkfm_exarch_scope
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Alexander Battenburg, the historical option
		name = balkfm.559.1
		default_option = yes
		scope:balkfm_battenburg_scope = {
			set_character_as_ruler = yes
			free_character_from_void = yes
		}
		balkfm_become_bulgaria_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = { # Emmanuel Bogoridi, grandson of Stefanos Bogoridi
		name = balkfm.559.2
		trigger = {
			has_variable = eocfm_is_autocephalous
		}
		scope:balkfm_bogoridi_scope = {
			set_character_as_ruler = yes
			free_character_from_void = yes
		}
		balkfm_become_bulgaria_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = { # Alexander Exarch, prominent Bulgarian revivalist
		name = balkfm.559.3
		trigger = {
			has_variable = balkfm_became_bulgaria_var
		}
		scope:balkfm_exarch_scope = {
			set_character_as_ruler = yes
			free_character_from_void = yes
		}
		balkfm_become_bulgaria_effect = yes
		remove_variable = balkfm_became_bulgaria_var
	}

}

balkfm.560 = { # Threats of Schism
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = balkfm.560.t
	desc = balkfm.560.d
	flavor = balkfm.560.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "southamerica_christianity"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_orthodox.dds"
	
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
	}
	
	immediate = {
		# triggered by balkfm.500
	}
	
	option = { # Declare Autocephaly
		name = balkfm.560.a
		default_option = yes
		add_modifier = modifier_eocfm_schismatic
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = eocfm_is_autocephalous
			}
			change_relations = {
				country = PREV
				value = -25
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_variable = eocfm_schism_var
				}
			}
			set_variable = {
				name = eocfm_schism_var
				value = 0
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Be a Soyboy
		name = balkfm.560.b
		add_modifier = {
			name = modifier_eocfm_autocephaly_abandoned
			months = long_modifier_time
		}
		add_radicals = {
			religion = rel:orthodox
			value = medium_radicals
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {

balkfm.561 = { # Royal Wedding; this is a chopped up version of PDX's vanilla wedding event
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = wedding.1.t
	desc = wedding.1.d
	flavor = wedding.1.f
	
	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:royal_marriage_princess
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_portrait.dds"
	
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
	}
	
	immediate = {
		create_character = {
			# Princess Marija of Montenegro, daughter of Nicholas I of Montenegro, died in infancy historically
			first_name = Marija
			last_name = Petrovic_Njegos
			historical = yes
			age = 18 # would have been 14 in 1883, so uhh, yeah
			female = yes
			culture = cu:serb
			religion = rel:orthodox
			interest_group = ig_landowners
			traits = {
				reserved
			}
			on_created = {	
				set_variable = balkfm_is_marija
				set_variable = getting_married
				place_character_in_void = 720 # 60 year lease on life
			}
		}
		random_character_in_void = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = balkfm_is_marija
			}
			save_scope_as = royal_marriage_princess
		}
		ruler = {
			save_scope_as = royal_marriage_character
		}
		capital = {
			save_scope_as = capital_scope
		}
		c:MON = {
			save_scope_as = marriage_country
			ruler = {
				save_scope_as = foreign_ruler
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # private wedding for international nobility
		name = wedding.1.a
		default_option = yes
		add_modifier = { # influence mult
			name = royal_marriage
			months = normal_modifier_time
		}
	}
	
	option = { # public wedding for the masses
		name = wedding.1.b
		scope:royal_marriage_character = {
			add_modifier = { # popularity
				name = marriage_popularity
				months = very_long_modifier_time
			}
		}
	}
	
	after = {
		scope:royal_marriage_character = {
			remove_variable = getting_married
		}
	}
}

balkfm.563 = { # An Orthodox Heir
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = balkfm.563.t
	desc = balkfm.563.d
	flavor = balkfm.563.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "votp_monarch_holding_court"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_orthodox.dds"
	
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_variable = eocfm_ruler_conversion_considered
		}
		has_law = law_type:law_monarchy
		ruler = {
			NOT = {
				has_religion = orthodox
			}
		}
		heir ?= {
			NOT = {
				has_religion = orthodox
			}
		}
		ig:ig_devout = {
			ig_approval <= 5
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_variable = eocfm_ruler_conversion_considered
		ruler = {
			save_scope_as = eocfm_ruler_scope
		}
		heir = {
			save_scope_as = eocfm_heir_scope
		}
	}	
	
	option = { # Both will convert
		name = balkfm.563.a
		default_option = yes
		scope:eocfm_ruler_scope = {
			change_character_religion = rel:orthodox
			add_modifier = modifier_eocfm_accepted_conversion
		}
		scope:eocfm_heir_scope = {
			change_character_religion = rel:orthodox
			add_modifier = modifier_eocfm_accepted_conversion
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = modifier_eocfm_ruler_accepted_conversion
			months = normal_modifier_time
		}
		add_loyalists = {
			religion = rel:orthodox
			value = medium_radicals
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				country_has_state_religion = rel:catholic
			}
			change_relations = {
				country = root
				value = -25
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				country_has_state_religion = rel:orthodox
			}
			change_relations = {
				country = root
				value = 25
			}
		}
		c:RUS ?= {
			set_secret_goal = {
				country = root
				secret_goal = protect
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Heir will convert
		name = balkfm.563.b
		scope:eocfm_ruler_scope = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_eocfm_refused_conversion
				months = very_long_modifier_time
			}
		}
		scope:eocfm_heir_scope = {
			change_character_religion = rel:orthodox
			add_modifier = modifier_eocfm_accepted_conversion
		}
		add_loyalists = {
			religion = rel:orthodox
			value = small_radicals
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				country_has_state_religion = rel:catholic
			}
			change_relations = {
				country = root
				value = -15
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				country_has_state_religion = rel:orthodox
			}
			change_relations = {
				country = root
				value = 15
			}
		}
		c:RUS ?= {
			set_secret_goal = {
				country = root
				secret_goal = befriend
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # I mean, isn't this just the eocfm choice but worse?
		name = balkfm.563.c
		scope:eocfm_ruler_scope = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_eocfm_refused_conversion
				months = very_long_modifier_time
			}
		}
		scope:eocfm_heir_scope = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_eocfm_refused_conversion
				months = very_long_modifier_time
			}
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = modifier_eocfm_ruler_refused_conversion
			months = long_modifier_time
		}
		add_radicals = {
			religion = rel:orthodox
			value = large_radicals
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				country_has_state_religion = rel:catholic
			}
			change_relations = {
				country = root
				value = 15
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				country_has_state_religion = rel:orthodox
			}
			change_relations = {
				country = root
				value = -15
			}
		}
		c:AUS ?= {
			set_secret_goal = {
				country = root
				secret_goal = protect
			}
		}
	}

}

balkfm.578 = { # Eastern Rumelia Rebels!
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = balkfm.578.t
	desc = balkfm.578.d
	flavor = balkfm.578.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "votp_agitator_speaking"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_fire.dds"
	
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		# triggered by balkfm_uplift_rumelia_button
	}
	
	immediate = { # As if there aren't enough events all trying to hammer this type of effect
		if = {
			limit = {
				c:TUR ?= this
			}
			create_country = {
				tag = ERUM
				origin = this
				state = s:STATE_NORTHERN_THRACE.region_state:TUR
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_country_type = recognized
				}
				create_diplomatic_pact = {
					country = c:ERUM
					type = dominion
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					is_country_type = unrecognized
				}
				create_diplomatic_pact = {
					country = c:ERUM
					type = vassal
				}
			}
		}
		c:ERUM ?= {
			save_scope_as = rumelia_scope
		}
		c:TUR ?= {
			save_scope_as = ottoman_scope
		}
		c:BUL = {
			save_scope_as = bulgaria_scope
			trigger_event = {
				id = balkfm.578 # Eastern Rumelia Rebels!
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # For BUL
		name = balkfm.578.a
		default_option = yes
		change_relations = {
			country = c:ERUM
			value = 50
		}
	}
	
	option = { # For TUR, spank them!
		name = balkfm.578.b
		scope:rumelia_scope = {
			make_independent = yes
		}
		create_diplomatic_play = {
			name = eqfm_balkan_rebellion
			target_country = scope:rumelia_scope
			type = dp_secession
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random_diplomatic_play = {
				limit = {
					c:TUR = {
						is_diplomatic_play_initiator = yes
					}
					scope:rumelia_scope = {
						is_diplomatic_play_target = yes
					}
				}
				add_diplomatic_play_war_support = { target = scope:rumelia_scope value = 100 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # For TUR, be a pansy...
		name = balkfm.578.c
		scope:rumelia_scope = {
			increase_autonomy = yes
		}
		create_bidirectional_truce = {  
			country = scope:rumelia_scope
			months = 60
		}
		add_radicals = {
			culture = cu:turkish
			value = medium_radicals
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = modifier_eqfm_caved_to_separatists
			months = normal_modifier_time
		}
	}

}

balkfm.598 = { # The Bulgarian State
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = balkfm.598.t
	desc = balkfm.598.d
	flavor = balkfm.598.f
	
	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:bulgaria_ruler_scope
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_bulgaria.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_global_variable = balkfm_bulgaria_tag_switch_accepted }
		has_global_variable = eqfm_berlin_congress_completed
		NOT = { has_global_variable = balkfm_bulgaria_tag_switch_technical }
		NOT = { has_variable = balkfm_bulgaria_tag_switch_offered }
		is_player = yes
		has_diplomatic_relevance = c:BUL
		c:BUL ?= {
			is_ai = yes
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_global_variable = balkfm_bulgaria_tag_switch_technical # this is in case we have multiple players
		set_variable = balkfm_bulgaria_tag_switch_offered
		c:BUL = {
			save_scope_as = bulgaria_scope
			ruler = {
				save_scope_as = bulgaria_ruler_scope
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Do Nothing
		name = balkfm.598.a
		default_option = yes
		remove_global_variable = balkfm_bulgaria_tag_switch_technical
	}
	
	option = { # Play as BUL
		name = balkfm.598.b
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_variable = balkfm_lion_awakened # checking for balkfm.500
				}
				c:BUL = {
					trigger_event = {
						id = balkfm.599 # The Golden Lion Awakens (Alternate)
						days = 1 # to prevent the AI from auto-resolving the event
					}
				}
			}
		}
		set_global_variable = balkfm_bulgaria_tag_switch_accepted
		remove_global_variable = balkfm_bulgaria_tag_switch_technical
		play_as = c:BUL
	}

}

balkfm.601 = { # The Petition-Proclamation
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = balkfm.601.t
	desc = balkfm.601.d
	flavor = balkfm.601.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "africa_leader_arguing"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_portrait.dds"
	
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		c:MOL ?= this
		NOT = { has_variable = balkfm_1848_happened }
		has_global_variable = peoples_springtime_happening
		NOT = { has_global_variable = peoples_springtime_happened }
		has_technology_researched = romanticism
	}	
	
	immediate = {
		set_variable = balkfm_1848_happened
		balkfm_set_up_1848_variables_effect = yes
		create_character = {
			# Vasile Alecsandri, Romanian nationalist and radical
			template = template_balkfm_alecsandri_vasile
			on_created = {
				set_variable = balkfm_is_revolutionary
				place_character_in_void = 12 # just for this event
			}
		}
		create_character = {
			# Ion Isăcescu, Romanian statesman and argonomist
			template = template_balkfm_isacescu_ion
			on_created = {
				set_variable = balkfm_is_revolutionary
				place_character_in_void = 12 # just for this event
			}
		}
		random_character_in_void = {
			limit = {
				has_template = template_balkfm_alecsandri_vasile
			}
			save_scope_as = balkfm_alecsandri_scope
		}
		random_character_in_void = {
			limit = {
				has_template = template_balkfm_isacescu_ion
			}
			save_scope_as = balkfm_isacescu_scope
		}
		ig:ig_landowners = {
			leader = {
				save_scope_as = balkfm_landowner_leader_scope
			}
		}
		ruler = {
			save_scope_as = balkfm_ruler_scope
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Resist the Proclamation
		name = balkfm.601.a
		default_option = yes
		scope:balkfm_ruler_scope = {
			set_ideology = ideology:ideology_royalist
		}
		scope:balkfm_alecsandri_scope = {
			free_character_from_void = yes
			set_as_interest_group_leader = yes
			set_ideology = ideology:ideology_radical
		}
		scope:balkfm_isacescu_scope = {
			free_character_from_void = yes
			set_as_interest_group_leader = yes
		}
		add_radicals = {
			pop_type = academics
			value = medium_radicals
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Accept the Proclamation
		name = balkfm.601.b
		scope:balkfm_ruler_scope = {
			set_ideology = ideology:ideology_humanitarian_royalist
		}
		scope:balkfm_landowner_leader_scope = {
			set_ideology = ideology:ideology_authoritarian
		}
		scope:balkfm_alecsandri_scope = {
			free_character_from_void = yes
			set_as_interest_group_leader = yes
			set_ideology = ideology:ideology_social_democrat
		}
		scope:balkfm_isacescu_scope = {
			free_character_from_void = yes
			set_as_interest_group_leader = yes
		}
		add_radicals = {
			pop_type = aristocrats
			value = medium_radicals
		}
	}
	
	after = {
		trigger_event = {
			id = balkfm.602 # The Moldavian Revolutionary Committee
			days = 30
		}
	}

}

balkfm.603 = { # Kogălniceanu's Revolution
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = balkfm.603.t
	desc = balkfm.603.d
	flavor = balkfm.603.f

	}

	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
	}	
	
	immediate = {
		balkfm_find_kogalniceanu_effect = yes
		c:RUS = {
			save_scope_as = russia_scope
		}
		c:TUR = {
			save_scope_as = ottoman_scope
		}
		c:MOL = {
			save_scope_as = moldavia_scope
		}
		heir = {
			save_scope_as = balkfm_heir_scope
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = balkfm.603.a
		default_option = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = modifier_balkfm_liberal_vanguard
			months = normal_modifier_time
		}		
		scope:balkfm_kogalniceanu_scope = {
			free_character_from_void = yes
			set_as_interest_group_leader = yes # Vasile Alecsandri left Moldavia after the attempted revolution
			set_character_as_ruler = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_law = law_type:law_autocracy
					has_law = law_type:law_oligarchy
				}
			}
			activate_law = law_type:law_landed_voting
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:balkfm_heir_scope ?= {
				kill_character = yes
			}
		}
		set_variable = balkfm_1848_succeeded
	}

			save_scope_as = moldavia_scope
		}

			save_scope_as = wallachia_scope
		}
		c:RUS = {
			save_scope_as = russia_scope
		}

	}

			days = 30
		}

balkfm.611 = { # Proclamation of Islaz
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = balkfm.611.t
	desc = balkfm.611.d
	flavor = balkfm.611.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "africa_leader_arguing"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_newspaper.dds"
	
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		c:WAL ?= this
		NOT = { has_variable = balkfm_1848_happened }
		has_global_variable = peoples_springtime_happening
		NOT = { has_global_variable = peoples_springtime_happened }
		has_technology_researched = romanticism
	}	
	
	immediate = {
		set_variable = balkfm_1848_happened
		balkfm_set_up_1848_variables_effect = yes
		create_character = {
			# Nicolae Bălcescu, leader of the 1848 revolution
			template = template_balkfm_balcescu_nicolae
			on_created = {
				set_variable = balkfm_is_revolutionary
				place_character_in_void = 12 # just for this event
			}
		}
		create_character = {
			# Alexandru G. Golescu, prominent boyar member of the brotherhood
			template = template_balkfm_golescu_alexandru
			on_created = {
				set_variable = balkfm_is_revolutionary
				place_character_in_void = 12 # just for this event
			}
		}
		create_character = {
			# Neofit Gianoglu, Metropolitan of Wallachia 1840-1849
			template = template_balkfm_gianoglu_neofit
			on_created = {
				set_variable = balkfm_is_revolutionary
				place_character_in_void = 12 # just for this event
			}
		}
		create_character = {
			# Christian Tell, major general and member of the brotherhood
			template = template_balkfm_tell_christian
			on_created = {
				set_variable = balkfm_is_revolutionary
				place_character_in_void = 12 # just for this event
			}
		}
		random_character_in_void = {
			limit = {
				has_template = template_balkfm_balcescu_nicolae
			}
			save_scope_as = balkfm_balcescu_scope
		}
		random_character_in_void = {
			limit = {
				has_template = template_balkfm_golescu_alexandru
			}
			save_scope_as = balkfm_golsecu_scope
		}
		random_character_in_void = {
			limit = {
				has_template = template_balkfm_gianoglu_neofit
			}
			save_scope_as = balkfm_gianoglu_scope
		}
		random_character_in_void = {
			limit = {
				has_template = template_balkfm_tell_christian
			}
			save_scope_as = balkfm_tell_scope
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Support the Rebels
		name = balkfm.611.a
		default_option = yes
		ruler = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_balkfm_receptive_domnitor
				months = very_long_modifier_time
			}
		}
		scope:balkfm_balcescu_scope = {
			free_character_from_void = yes
			set_as_interest_group_leader = yes
		}
		scope:balkfm_golsecu_scope = {
			free_character_from_void = yes
			set_as_interest_group_leader = yes
		}
		scope:balkfm_gianoglu_scope = {
			free_character_from_void = yes
			set_as_interest_group_leader = yes
		}
		scope:balkfm_tell_scope = {
			free_character_from_void = yes
			set_as_interest_group_leader = yes
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Do Not
		name = balkfm.611.b
		ruler = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_balkfm_unreceptive_domnitor
				months = very_long_modifier_time
			}
		}
		scope:balkfm_balcescu_scope = {
			free_character_from_void = yes
			set_as_interest_group_leader = yes
		}
		scope:balkfm_golsecu_scope = {
			set_ideology = ideology:ideology_radical
			free_character_from_void = yes
			set_as_interest_group_leader = yes
		}
		scope:balkfm_gianoglu_scope = {
			set_ideology = ideology:ideology_authoritarian
			free_character_from_void = yes
			set_as_interest_group_leader = yes
		}
		scope:balkfm_tell_scope = {
			free_character_from_void = yes
			set_as_interest_group_leader = yes
		}
	}
	
	after = {
		trigger_event = {
			id = balkfm.612 # The Wallachian Brotherhood
			days = 30
		}
	}

}

	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				has_template = template_balkfm_balcescu_nicolae
			}
			save_scope_as = balkfm_balcescu_scope
		}
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				has_template = template_balkfm_gianoglu_neofit
			}

		}
	}

balkfm.624 = { # Electing a Hospodar (MOL)
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = balkfm.624.t
	desc = balkfm.624.d
	flavor = balkfm.624.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "unspecific_politicians_arguing"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_newspaper.dds"
	
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		var:balkfm_regulamentul_var <= 0
		c:MOL ?= this
		NOT = { has_variable = balkfm_1848_rom_var }
	}
	
	immediate = {
		change_variable = {
			name = balkfm_hospodar_election_counter
			add = 1
		}		
		set_variable = {
			name = balkfm_regulamentul_var
			value = 7
		}
		balkfm_moldavian_election_effect = yes
		ruler = {
			save_scope_as = balkfm_hospodar_candidate_1
		}
		random_character_in_void = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = balkfm_hospodar_m1
			}
			save_scope_as = balkfm_hospodar_candidate_2
		}
		random_character_in_void = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = balkfm_hospodar_m2
			}
			save_scope_as = balkfm_hospodar_candidate_3
		}
		heir ?= {
			save_scope_as = balkfm_heir_scope
		}
	}
	
	option = { # keep current ruler
		name = balkfm.624.a
		default_option = yes
		scope:balkfm_hospodar_candidate_1 = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_balkfm_tenure_extended
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # historical successor
		name = balkfm.624.b
		scope:balkfm_hospodar_candidate_2 = {
			free_character_from_void = yes
			set_character_as_ruler = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:balkfm_heir_scope ?= {
				kill_character = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # alternate successor
		name = balkfm.624.c
		scope:balkfm_hospodar_candidate_3 = {
			free_character_from_void = yes
			set_character_as_ruler = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:balkfm_heir_scope ?= {
				kill_character = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	after = {
		ruler = {
			remove_variable = balkfm_hospodar_m1
			remove_variable = balkfm_hospodar_m2
			remove_variable = balkfm_hospodar_w1
			remove_variable = balkfm_hospodar_w2
		}
	}

}

		}
	}
	
	option = { # alternate successor
		name = balkfm.625.c
		scope:balkfm_hospodar_candidate_3 = {
			free_character_from_void = yes
			set_character_as_ruler = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:balkfm_heir_scope ?= {
				kill_character = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	after = {
		ruler = {
			remove_variable = balkfm_hospodar_m1
			remove_variable = balkfm_hospodar_m2
			remove_variable = balkfm_hospodar_w1
			remove_variable = balkfm_hospodar_w2
		}
	}

}

balkfm.629 = { # A Monstrous Coalition
	type = country_event

	}

	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
	}	
	
	immediate = {
		set_variable = balkfm_dezvoltator_completed
		heir = {
			save_scope_as = balkfm_heir_scope
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Carol I -  the historical option
		name = balkfm.629.a
		default_option = yes
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = balkfm.629.a.tt
			hidden_effect = {
				create_character = {
					template = template_balkfm_karl_hohenzollern
					on_created = {
						set_character_as_ruler = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		trigger_event = {
			id = balkfm.640 # An Elected Domnitor
			days = 30
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Philippe de Flandre - the Belgian option; from grefm.009
		name = balkfm.629.b
		trigger = {
			c:BEL ?= {
				has_diplomatic_pact = {
					who = root
					type = alliance
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				has_global_variable = grefm_the_belgian_option
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = balkfm.629.b.tt
			hidden_effect = {
				create_character = {
					template = template_grefm_deflandre_philippe
					on_created = {
						set_character_as_ruler = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		trigger_event = {
			id = balkfm.640 # An Elected Domnitor
			days = 30
		}
		set_global_variable = grefm_the_belgian_option # blocks this option on the grefm side

	}
	
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					exists = scope:balkfm_heir_scope
				}
				scope:balkfm_heir_scope = {
					kill_character = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

}

balkfm.641 = { # Liberalist Demands
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = balkfm.641.t
	desc = balkfm.641.d
	flavor = balkfm.641.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "unspecific_politicians_arguing"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_scales.dds"
	
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		# triggered by balkfm.641
	}	
	
	immediate = {
		set_variable = balkfm_1866_technical
	}
	
	option = { # Accept the Constitution
		name = balkfm.641.a
		default_option = yes
		if = { # It doesn't make sense to add the journal if it's completion conditions are met
			limit = {
				AND = {
					OR = {
						has_law = law_type:law_wealth_voting
						has_law = law_type:law_census_voting
						has_law = law_type:law_universal_suffrage
					}
					OR = {
						has_law = law_type:law_freedom_of_conscience
						has_law = law_type:law_total_separation
					}
					OR = {
						has_law = law_type:law_right_of_assembly
						has_law = law_type:law_protected_speech
					}
					OR = {
						has_law = law_type:law_commercialized_agriculture
						has_law = law_type:law_homesteading
					}
				}
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_balkfm_democratic_constitution
				months = long_modifier_time
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_journal_entry = {
				type = je_balkfm_rom_1866_1
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # How About Nope-stitution
		name = balkfm.641.b
		balkfm_initialize_1866_variables_effect = yes
		add_journal_entry = {
			type = je_balkfm_rom_1866_2
		}
	}
	
	after = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = balkfm_1866_var
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = balkfm_1866_var
				add = 100
			}
		}
		remove_variable = balkfm_1866_technical
	}

}

balkfm.642 = { # A Conspiracy in Ploiești
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = balkfm.642.t
	desc = balkfm.642.d
	flavor = balkfm.642.f
	
	event_image = {
		video = "votp_conspiring"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_protest.dds"
	
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_variable = balkfm_ploiesti_happened }
		var:balkfm_1866_var < 75
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_variable = balkfm_ploiesti_happened
		create_character = {
			template = template_balkfm_candiano_alexandru
			on_created = {
				place_character_in_void = 700
			}
		}
		random_character_in_void = {
			limit = {
				has_template = template_balkfm_candiano_alexandru
			}
			save_scope_as = balkfm_candiano_scope
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Arrest These Idiots
		name = balkfm.642.a
		default_option = yes
		scope:balkfm_candiano_scope = {
			free_character_from_void = yes
			exile_character = yes
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = balkfm.642.tt
			hidden_effect = {
				change_variable = {
					name = balkfm_1866_var
					subtract = 20
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					trigger_event = {
						id = balkfm.643 # Ploiești Revolt Suppressed
					}
				}
				50 = {
					trigger_event = {
						id = balkfm.644 # Ploieștian Radicalism Spreads
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Cave to Their Demands
		name = balkfm.642.b
		scope:balkfm_candiano_scope = {
			free_character_from_void = yes
			set_as_interest_group_leader = yes
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = modifier_balkfm_ploiesti_succeeded
			months = long_modifier_time
		}
		ruler = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_balkfm_impotent_ruler
				months = long_modifier_time
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_law = law_type:law_autocracy
					has_law = law_type:law_oligarchy
					has_law = law_type:law_landed_voting
					has_law = law_type:law_wealth_voting
					has_law = law_type:law_census_voting
				}
			}
			activate_law = law_type:law_universal_suffrage
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_law = law_type:law_serfdom
					has_law = law_type:law_tenant_farmers
				}
			}
			activate_law = law_type:law_homesteading
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_law = law_type:law_consumption_based_taxation
					has_law = law_type:law_land_based_taxation
				}
			}
			activate_law = law_type:law_per_capita_based_taxation 
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Give This Moron a Job
		name = balkfm.642.c
		scope:balkfm_candiano_scope = {
			free_character_from_void = yes
			transfer_character = root
			add_character_role = general
			set_ideology = ideology:ideology_reformer
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				80 = {
					trigger_event = {
						id = balkfm.643 # Ploiești Revolt Suppressed
						popup = yes
					}
				}
				20 = {
					trigger_event = {
						id = balkfm.644 # Ploieștian Radicalism Spreads
						days = 30
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	left_icon = scope:balkfm_mairoescu_scope
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_portrait.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		# triggered by je_balkfm_rom_nationalism
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_variable = balkfm_romanian_nationalism_started
		balkfm_calculate_protochronism_effect = yes
		create_character = {
			# Titu Maiorescu, de facto leader of the Junimea society
			template = template_balkfm_mairoescu_titu
			on_created = {
				place_character_in_void = 12 # just for this event
			}
		}
		random_character_in_void = {
			limit = {
				has_template = template_balkfm_mairoescu_titu
			}
			save_scope_as = balkfm_mairoescu_scope
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = balkfm.670.a
		default_option = yes
		scope:balkfm_mairoescu_scope = {
			free_character_from_void = yes
			set_as_interest_group_leader = yes
		}
	}
	
	after = {
		balkfm_calculate_protochronism_effect = yes
		trigger_event = {
			id = balkfm.671 # Etymologicum Magnum Romaniae
			days = 90
		}
	}

}

		}

			name = modifier_balkfm_dacianist_society
			months = long_modifier_time
		}

		}

	}

#### ROMANIAN UNIFICATION EVENTS ####

balkfm.680 = { # Our Declaration of Union (romania.2, integrated into balkfm)
	type = country_event

	title = balkfm.680.t
	desc = balkfm.680.d
	flavor = balkfm.680.f

	event_image = {
		video = "unspecific_ruler_speaking_to_people"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/waving_flag.dds"

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
        random_country = {
        	limit = {
	        	NOT = { this = ROOT }
	        	country_has_primary_culture = cu:romanian
	            relations:root >= 25
	            OR = {
	            	AND = {
	            		exists = top_overlord
						is_subject = yes
						top_overlord = {
							THIS = root.top_overlord
						}
					}
					is_subject = no
	            }
        	}
        	save_scope_as = romania_lesser_partner
        	set_variable = {
        		name = romania_union_partner
        	}
        }
		if = { # this goes in the immediate because of the simplified variables
			limit = {
				has_law = law_type:law_monarchy
				scope:romania_lesser_partner = {
					has_law = law_type:law_monarchy
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = balkfm.680.a.tta
				create_diplomatic_pact = {
					country = scope:romania_lesser_partner
					type = personal_union
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = balkfm.680.a.ttb
				create_diplomatic_pact = {
					country = scope:romania_lesser_partner
					type = puppet
				}
			}
		}
    }

	option = { # je_all_for_one is out in order to bring the entire event chain under balkfm control; this should make this compatible with VTM since it knocks out all romania content
		name = balkfm.680.a
		default_option = yes
		show_as_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_law = law_type:law_monarchy
					scope:romania_lesser_partner = {
						has_law = law_type:law_monarchy
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = {
					text = balkfm.680.a.tta
					create_diplomatic_pact = {
						country = scope:romania_lesser_partner
						type = personal_union
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				custom_tooltip = {
					text = balkfm.680.a.ttb
					create_diplomatic_pact = {
						country = scope:romania_lesser_partner
						type = puppet
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

balkfm.681 = { # Awaken Thee, Romanian! (romania.3, integrated into balkfm)
	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT
	title = balkfm.681.t
	desc = {
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = {
				desc = balkfm.681.d2
				trigger = {
					exists = c:TRS
					any_subject_or_below = {
						c:TRS = this
					}
				}
			}
			triggered_desc = {
				desc = balkfm.681.d
				trigger = {
					NOT = {
						any_subject_or_below = {
							c:TRS = this
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	flavor =  balkfm.681.f

	duration = 3

	event_image = {
		video = "unspecific_military_parade"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_default.dds"

	trigger = {
		# triggered by JE
	}

	immediate = {
        random_neighbouring_state = {
            limit = {
                owner = {
                    has_variable = romania_union_partner
                }
            }
            owner = {
                save_scope_as = romania_lesser_union_partner
            }
        }
        if = {
        	limit = {
	        	exists = c:TRS
	        	c:TRS = {
	        		is_subject_of = ROOT
	        	}
	        }
	        c:TRS = {
	        	save_scope_as = transylvania_union_partner
	        }
        }
		set_variable = {
			name = balkfm_junimism_var
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			name = balkfm_dacianism_var
			value = 0
		}
	}

	option = { # Unite Romania
		name = balkfm.681.a
		default_option = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:romania_lesser_union_partner = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
					is_player = no
				}
			}
			annex = scope:romania_lesser_union_partner
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				c:TRS ?= {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
					is_player = no
				}
			}
			annex = c:TRS
		}
		change_tag = ROM
	}

}

		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOR = 
					{ owns_entire_state_region = STATE_BESSARABIA }
					has_claim = s:STATE_BESSARABIA
			}
			s:STATE_BESSARABIA = {
				add_claim = ROOT
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOR = 
					{ owns_entire_state_region = STATE_BEKES }
					has_claim = s:STATE_BEKES
			}
			s:STATE_BEKES = {
				add_claim = ROOT
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOR = 
					{ owns_entire_state_region = STATE_MOLDAVIA }
					has_claim = s:STATE_MOLDAVIA
			}
			s:STATE_MOLDAVIA = {
				add_claim = ROOT
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOR = 
					{ owns_entire_state_region = STATE_NORTHERN_TRANSYLVANIA }
					has_claim = s:STATE_NORTHERN_TRANSYLVANIA
			}
			s:STATE_NORTHERN_TRANSYLVANIA = {
				add_claim = ROOT
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOR = 
					{ owns_entire_state_region = STATE_SOUTHERN_TRANSYLVANIA }
					has_claim = s:STATE_SOUTHERN_TRANSYLVANIA
			}
			s:STATE_SOUTHERN_TRANSYLVANIA = {
				add_claim = ROOT
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {

					{ owns_entire_state_region = STATE_WALLACHIA }
					has_claim = s:STATE_WALLACHIA
			}
			s:STATE_WALLACHIA = {
				add_claim = ROOT
			}
		}
	}

}

balkfm.900 = { # Illyrian Sentiment
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = balkfm.900.t
	desc = balkfm.900.d
	flavor = balkfm.900.f
	
	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:balkfm_draskovic_scope
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_croatia.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		# triggered from GLOBAL
	}
	
	cancellation_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_journal_entry = je_balkfm_cro_croation_question
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_character_in_void = {
			limit = {
				has_template = template_balkfm_draskovic_janko
			}
			save_scope_as = balkfm_draskovic_scope
		}
		ig:ig_landowners = {
			leader = {
				save_scope_as = balkfm_metternich_scope
			}
		}
		c:TUR = {
			save_scope_as = ottoman_scope
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = balkfm.900.a
		default_option = yes
		every_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				state_region = {
					is_homeland = cu:croat
				}
			}
			add_modifier = modifier_balkfm_croatian_revivalism
		}
		add_radicals = {
			culture = cu:croat
			value = medium_radicals
		}
	}

}

balkfm.901 = { # An Austro-Slavic Proposal
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = balkfm.901.t
	desc = balkfm.901.d
	flavor = balkfm.901.f
	
	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:balkfm_borovsky_scope
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_portrait.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/misc/1Character_Banner"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_variable = balkfm_austro_slavic_proposal_var
		}
		has_technology_researched = nationalism
	}
	
	cancellation_trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_journal_entry = je_balkfm_cro_croation_question
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_variable = balkfm_austro_slavic_proposal_var
		create_character = {
			template = template_balkfm_borovsky_karel
			on_created = {
				place_character_in_void = 12
			}
		}
		random_character_in_void = {
			limit = {
				has_template = template_balkfm_borovsky_karel
			}
			save_scope_as = balkfm_borovsky_scope
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Support the Proposal
		name = balkfm.901.a
		default_option = yes
		add_radicals = {
			culture = cu:hungarian
			value = medium_radicals
		}
		balkfm_happy_yugoslavs_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = { # Oppose the Proposal
		name = balkfm.901.b
		add_loyalists = {
			culture = cu:hungarian
			value = medium_radicals
		}
		balkfm_sad_yugoslavs_effect = yes
	}

}

balkfm.909 = { # Croatian–Hungarian Settlement / Austro-Croatian Compromise
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	
	title = {
		triggered_desc = {
			desc = balkfm.909.t1
			trigger = {
				country_has_primary_culture = cu:hungarian
			}
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			desc = balkfm.909.t2
			trigger = {
				NOT = {
					country_has_primary_culture = cu:hungarian
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		triggered_desc = {
			desc = balkfm.909.d1
			trigger = {
				country_has_primary_culture = cu:hungarian
				NOT = {
					has_variable = balkfm_croatian_question_failed
				}
			}
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			desc = balkfm.909.d2
			trigger = {
				NOR = {
					country_has_primary_culture = cu:hungarian
					has_variable = balkfm_croatian_question_failed
				}
			}
		}
	}
	flavor = {
		triggered_desc = {
			desc = balkfm.909.f1
			trigger = {
				NOT = {
					has_variable = balkfm_croatian_question_failed
				}
			}
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			desc = balkfm.909.f2
			trigger = {
				has_variable = balkfm_croatian_question_failed
			}
		}
	}
	
	event_image = {
		video = "votp_monarch_holding_court"
	}
	
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_croatia.dds"
	
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	
	duration = 3
	
	dlc = dlc_grefm
	
	trigger = {
		# triggered by je_balkfm_cro_croation_question
	}
	
	cancellation_trigger = {
		NOR = {
			any_scope_state = {
				state_region = {
					is_homeland = cu:croat
				}
			}
			c:CRO ?= {
				is_subject_of = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_variable = balkfm_croatian_question_complete
	}
	
	## Croatian–Hungarian Settlement Options ##
	
	option = { # Success Option
		name = balkfm.909.a1
		default_option = yes
		trigger = {
			country_has_primary_culture = cu:hungarian
			NOR = {
				has_variable = balkfm_croatian_question_failed
				c:CRO ?= {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		add_primary_culture = cu:croat
		add_loyalists = {
			culture = cu:croat
			value = large_radicals
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Success Option, if Croatia is a subject
		name = balkfm.909.a2
		default_option = yes
		trigger = {
			country_has_primary_culture = cu:hungarian
			NOT = {
				has_variable = balkfm_croatian_question_failed
			}
			c:CRO ?= {
				is_subject_of = ROOT
			}
		}
		c:CRO ?= {
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_balkfm_croatian_autonomy
				months = long_modifier_time
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Accept Compromise
		name = balkfm.909.a3
		trigger = {
			country_has_primary_culture = cu:hungarian
			has_variable = balkfm_croatian_question_failed
		}
		add_primary_culture = cu:croat
		add_loyalists = {
			culture = cu:croat
			value = large_radicals
		}
		add_radicals = {
			value = large_radicals
			culture = cu:hungarian
			pop_type = aristocrats
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = dual_monarchy_compromise
			months = very_long_modifier_time
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Reject Compromise
		name = balkfm.909.a4
		trigger = {
			country_has_primary_culture = cu:hungarian
			has_variable = balkfm_croatian_question_failed
		}
		add_radicals = {
			value = very_large_radicals
			culture = cu:croat
		}
		every_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				state_region = {
					is_homeland = cu:croat
				}
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_balkfm_croatian_compromise_rejected
				months = long_modifier_time
			}
		}
	}
	
	## Austro-Croatian Compromise Options ##
	
	option = { # Success Option
		name = balkfm.909.b1
		default_option = yes
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				country_has_primary_culture = cu:hungarian
				has_variable = balkfm_croatian_question_failed
				c:CRO ?= {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		add_primary_culture = cu:croat
		add_loyalists = {
			culture = cu:croat
			value = large_radicals
		}
		add_radicals = {
			value = large_radicals
			culture = cu:hungarian
			pop_type = aristocrats
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Success Option, if Croatia is a subject
		name = balkfm.909.b2
		default_option = yes
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				country_has_primary_culture = cu:hungarian
				has_variable = balkfm_croatian_question_failed
			}
			c:CRO ?= {
				is_subject_of = ROOT
			}
		}
		c:CRO ?= {
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_balkfm_croatian_autonomy
				months = long_modifier_time
			}
		}
		add_radicals = {
			value = large_radicals
			culture = cu:hungarian
			pop_type = aristocrats
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Accept Compromise
		name = balkfm.909.b3
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				country_has_primary_culture = cu:hungarian
			}
			has_variable = balkfm_croatian_question_failed
		}
		add_primary_culture = cu:croat
		add_loyalists = {
			culture = cu:croat
			value = large_radicals
		}
		add_radicals = {
			value = large_radicals
			culture = cu:south_german
			pop_type = aristocrats
		}
		add_radicals = {
			value = large_radicals
			culture = cu:hungarian
			pop_type = aristocrats
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = dual_monarchy_compromise
			months = very_long_modifier_time
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Reject Compromise
		name = balkfm.909.b4
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				country_has_primary_culture = cu:hungarian
			}
			has_variable = balkfm_croatian_question_failed
		}
		add_radicals = {
			value = very_large_radicals
			culture = cu:croat
		}
		add_loyalists = {
			value = large_radicals
			culture = cu:hungarian
			pop_type = aristocrats
		}
		every_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				state_region = {
					is_homeland = cu:croat
				}
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = modifier_balkfm_croatian_compromise_rejected
				months = long_modifier_time
			}
		}
	}

}

			}

				add_claim = ROOT
			}
		}

				add_claim = ROOT
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOR = {
					has_claim = s:STATE_DALMATIA

				}
			}
